Commentary

The Eighth Anniversary of the May 30th Incident - Zi

The May 30th Incident, which occupies an important position in the history of the Chinese national movement, has reached its eighth anniversary today. Recalling May 30th, 1925, the conflict between over a thousand people and dozens of police officers on Nanjing Road in Shanghai escalated into a tragedy with over twenty deaths and injuries. This led to a major strike throughout Shanghai. Furthermore, the Han, Xun, Yue, Yu, and Ning massacres followed one after another. The people of all China cooperated and fought together to complete a magnificent national movement. Its impact was that internally, it created the foundation for a national mass united revolution, and externally, it made the powerful countries have a considerable understanding of the awakening of the Chinese nation. Although the negotiations were not a complete victory, the historical course of the incident is enough to give the Chinese nation hope for its future.

The May 30th Incident was not just about the deaths and injuries of twenty-odd people, nor was it just about dealing with those directly responsible or a certain country. It was also not just a single incident that started with the labor unrest four months prior. It was a major movement for the Chinese nation to seek independence and survival. The reason for this was the decades of humiliation suffered by China externally and the history of active aggression against China by various countries. The basic substance was the acceptance of the global national movement by 400 million Chinese people, and the national will that was thus expressed. The result of this, up to eight years later, can be said not to have been obtained. Therefore, when we commemorate the incident, we should not focus on the temporary bloodshed tragedy, but should place importance on the background that created this bloodshed tragedy. We should not limit ourselves to mourning the martyrs of the May 30th Incident, but should consider how the independence and survival of the Chinese nation are threatened today.

Our people's resistance to Japan has reached the point where it has gone from the arduous struggles of the military and civilians to the authorities discussing a ceasefire today. Commemorating this incident, which demanded national independence and survival, is truly filled with grief and indignation. Although Japan's military capabilities are sufficient to temporarily occupy more than four provinces of our land, sufficient to destroy our hard-worked and unprotected villages and towns, sufficient to massacre the majority of our military and civilians whose resistance capabilities are not yet sufficient, and sufficient to pressure us into ceasefire negotiations on the front lines, they can never cut off the will of our entire nation to continue to struggle. If our nation can avoid falling into decline, can be inspired to become strong, and can continue to develop our national will, then there will be a day when the May 30th Incident, eight years ago, opened the end of our nation's struggle. From now on, we must follow the path to seek the elimination of threats to national independence and survival. The future is bright; let the people of the country move forward.

Since the Xinhai Revolution until the May 30th Incident, the number of people actually participating in the struggle in the Chinese national movement has increased daily, and the organization and capabilities have also expanded daily. Although the country targeted by the May 30th Incident did not show submission, it actually saw the opportunity and made concessions. If the Chinese national movement can continue to advance vigorously in the future, combining the strength of the entire nation and with tight organizations, then the final result will be sufficient to make those who infringe upon our independence and threaten our survival receive the lessons they deserve. The matter rests on the efforts of the people of the country.

Japan Fears Resistance to Goods

Ishii States in New York to Journalists

Will Submit Plans to Address at the Economic Conference

(New York) Ishii, the Japanese representative attending the World Economic Conference, arrived here today from Washington and told reporters that he will submit plans to address the Chinese policy of rejecting Japanese goods at the Economic Conference. Ishii pointed to Chinese resistance as the biggest obstacle in commerce and said that he already has a way to subdue Chinese resistance. He believes that resistance is an action that endangers the entire world, and he will submit his plan to the Economic Conference after it is drafted. (28th Reuters Dispatch)

Japanese Side Is Self-Satisfied

(Tokyo) The Ministry of Foreign Affairs believes that the meeting of representatives Ishii and Fukai with the US President in Washington had a major impact on the US government's new policy toward the Far East and is watching its progress with the utmost attention. The US President made it clear to representative Ishii that the Manchuria problem will no longer be discussed and that attention will be paid to promoting stability in the Far East in the future. The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs expressed satisfaction with this statement, namely that the United States hopes to cooperate with the Far East and Western countries and make an important foundation for world peace and prosperity policies, and to remove the current world unrest, advocates rational solutions to economic and transport reductions. It is different from the policies of previous US Republican governments. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs also recognizes this as a practical policy and is very satisfied. The Ministry believes that the results of this meeting between Japanese and American representatives will definitely improve the previous relationship between Japan and the United States and the entire relationship between China and Japan. (29th Nichiren Dispatch)

Ishii's Schedule in the United States

(New York) Ishii, Fukai and other plenipotentiaries arrived in New York from Washington at 4:00 PM today and immediately entered the Pierre Hotel for a meeting with the press corps. At 5:00 PM, they attended the welcome meeting of the Japanese Club's Consul General Horiuchi. Plenipotentiary Ishii is scheduled to broadcast a speech at 10:00 PM on the 29th, strongly advocating friendship between the United States and Japan, entitled "Departing from the United States". The 30th is a rest day. At 12:00 PM on the 31st, they will attend the official luncheon of lawyers at the Bar Association Club. At 2:00 PM, they will attend the invitation of the American Industrial Association and take a boat trip on the Hudson River. On June 1st, except for Plenipotentiary Fukai, the group will go to Boston and attend the dinner party of Ambassador to Japan Fokker Corpse. They will return to New York at 6:00 AM on the 2nd. The schedule in the United States will be completed here. On the afternoon of the 2nd, they will take the Olympic Wheel to London. (28th Dentsu Dispatch)

Japan Plans to Interfere with China's Tariff Autonomy

(Tokyo) The National Government implemented increased tariffs starting May 22nd. The Foreign Ministry instructed Consul-General Ishisha in Shanghai to investigate, as the tariffs have a significant impact on Japan's trade with China. It has been decided to lodge a protest with the National Government, and Minister Arima has been telegraphed with the following protest: "Your country's increase in tariffs has severely impacted Japanese trade and harmed friendly Sino-Japanese relations, which is deeply regrettable. We respectfully request reconsideration." (29th, Domei News Agency)

Report on Trade of National Goods in the Nanyang Islands

Tea Suffers from Taiwan Tea Dumping and Low Prices

Porcelain Industry Needs Improvement to Compete with Japanese Goods

(Singapore) The Chinese Consul-General in Singapore and other Chinese representatives in Nanyang have issued similar reports on the general situation of trade in Chinese products. The general gist is that items such as cotton cloth, leather suitcases, and flashlights are selling well and at reasonable prices. The high value of the Singapore dollar is favorable for Chinese products. However, Chinese tea has suffered a significant decline due to competition from Taiwanese tea. Taiwan currently ships 8 million kilograms of tea annually to Java and Sumatra, and 3 million kilograms to Malaya, while Chinese tea only ships 1 million kilograms to Java and Sumatra, and 500,000 kilograms to Malaya. Japanese porcelain has low prices and good designs, coupled with the low value of the Japanese yen, making it a competitor for the Chinese porcelain industry. Although Chinese merchants in this industry encourage overseas Chinese with patriotic appeals, the effect is limited, and it is ultimately difficult to compete with Japanese porcelain. Chinese manufactured goods have gained a foothold in the Dutch East Indies and British Malaya. The general situation in the past twelve months is considered good, but Chinese canned food has encountered setbacks because the supply and sale prices of fresh goods in various parts of Nanyang are already low. (29th, Reuters)

Russian Pravda Exposes Japan's Conspiracy to Invade China

Plans to Occupy Chahar Province in Hopes of Invading the Northwest

Seizing Railways in North China to Penetrate the Interior

Building Military Ports and Annexing the Yellow Sea

(Moscow) A commentary in the Pravda newspaper on the 27th stated that Japan is attempting to establish a new country in North China, similar to "Manchukuo," bounded by the Yellow River, and therefore cannot relax its grip on Shandong. Japan's objectives are threefold: (1) to turn Manchuria into a colony; (2) to establish administrative power in North China and gradually expand it to the entire country; and (3) to ultimately use the Chinese Empire to eliminate the Chinese Revolution. In the Northeast, it will inevitably further invade the Northwest. Its occupation of Chahar Province can be seen as a prelude to advancing north, west, and northwest. Progress in the northern direction will not provoke the opposition of Britain and the United States as much as invasion of the southwest. Therefore, it is a misunderstanding to say that Japan's aggression will end after it obtains the area north of the Great Wall. The newspaper also stated that what Japan pays particular attention to is the control of the railways of Liaoning-Tianjin, Ping-Zhangjiakou, and Baotou. If these railways are connected to the Pusan-Yang railways, the importance of their military and economic significance to Japan can be imagined. To the south of these railways are China's two major railways (referring to Tianjin-Pukou and Beijing-Hankou). To the west is the main road from Xinpukou to Beijing. By occupying these, Japan can not only extensively exploit all the resources of China but also have a base for penetrating China and Mongolia. The newspaper also stated that in order to secure transportation to North China and Hokkaido, Japan will establish administrative control over the Yellow River. Japan has built the Tsugaru naval base near Busan, and now it is restoring the Lushun military port. If Japan occupies Qingdao as a second base in the future, then the Yellow Sea will forever be without the shadow of national warships. Japan's various plans are related to preparations for war on the East Asian continent and war against the United States. (27th, Central News Agency)

Talk of Moving the World Economic Conference to Geneva

To Coordinate with the Disarmament Conference

British Proposal for Aerial Bombing Retains Reservations

Vehemently Criticized by Russian Representatives

(Geneva) The Secretariat of the League of Nations is currently working hard to move the venue of the World Economic Conference from London to Geneva. The biggest reason is that it is difficult to hope for the conclusion of the Disarmament Conference before the opening of the Economic Conference. Therefore, if the Economic Conference is to open on June 12th, it would be better to hold the two conferences in the same location, to avoid the dispersion and involvement of representatives from various countries. Furthermore, holding the two conferences in the same location can not only save time and economic resources but also bring many conveniences in terms of work. Moreover, the agreements reached at each conference can promote the progress of other conferences. (29th, National Telegram)

(Geneva) The British representative's request to retain the right to exercise "police powers" through bombing aircraft in "remote areas" was vehemently criticized by Soviet representative Stein today. Stein firmly insisted that Britain must remove Article 34 from its plan. It is said that we have not seen any government that has requested to exercise its police powers by aerial bombing over its people in remote areas, such as in colonies. The geographical term "remote areas" can be interpreted by any country as it pleases. Therefore, the Soviet delegation will in no way allow the retention of that part of Article 34 in the British plan. Regarding a certain country's representative's proposal to add the words "outside of Europe" to this reservation, Stein declared, "I do not understand why the people of continents outside of Europe should be specially granted the right to be bombed by aircraft." (27th, Tass)

(Geneva) French Foreign Minister Peng Gu has arrived in Geneva and will personally attend the General Committee of the Disarmament Conference. The committee will continue to discuss the definition of "aggressor" in the afternoon (29th, Havas)

(Geneva) Soviet Foreign Affairs Commissioner Litvinov is expected to arrive in Geneva tomorrow, Tuesday. (29th, Havas)

(Tokyo) According to a report from the Matsudaira Embassy in the United Kingdom, after the World Economic Conference opens in London on June 12th, it will be moved to Geneva. The Japanese Foreign Ministry has expressed great dissatisfaction with this report. Since Geneva is the place where Japan broke with the League of Nations, Japan is unwilling to participate in world conferences there again. Moreover, since its purpose is to conduct the Disarmament and Economic Conferences simultaneously, Japan, although participating in the Economic Conference to overcome domestic economic difficulties and hoping that the conference can achieve its goals, does not want to be interfered with by the world regarding disarmament issues because its continental policy has not been completed. It is heard that Foreign Minister Uchida will order the ambassadors stationed in the major powers of Britain, the United States, France, Germany, and Italy to vehemently oppose it. (29th, China United News Agency)

(Geneva) The Special Committee on Armaments of the Disarmament Conference met this morning. French representative Jouart made strong remarks, stating that the French delegation will immediately submit a proposal to the Presidium of the General Assembly in the form of amendments, as an annex to the British Disarmament Plan, advocating for the restriction of national defense expenditures and the crackdown on the public and private manufacturing industries of armaments and bullets. The purpose of the French proposal is to resist the means used by the majority of countries in the committee who do not support the restriction of national defense budgets and do not advocate for the supervision of the manufacture of armaments, and who strive to quickly conclude a convention, hoping to disregard these issues. (29th, Havas)

Four-Power Pact Negotiations Take a Sudden Turn for the Better

Signing Expected in Geneva

(Paris) Messages from London, Rome, and Geneva received by the Morning Post today stated that the Four-Power Pact is on the verge of being concluded and that the signing is expected to take place this week. The reason for this rapid conclusion is that Britain has agreed to incorporate Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant concerning sanctions into the pact. The Little Entente countries have also accepted French Foreign Minister Peng Gu's promise to conclude a separate treaty guaranteeing the security of the smaller countries, thereby abandoning their initial protests. (28th, National Telegram)

National Government Memorial Week

(Nanjing) The National Government held its weekly memorial ceremony on the morning of the 29th. Attending were Ye Chucang, Wei Huai, Lu Chao, Tang Shengzhi, He Yaozu, Chen Qicai, Li Yuanding, Zhang Daofan, Zhou Yawei, and over 300 civil and military officials. Chairman Ye Chucang presided over the ceremony and gave a report, emphasizing "frugality to save the nation." He stated that in this time of national crisis, we should dedicate all that we have to the nation to meet its needs. Colleagues in the National Government recently formed a Frugality to Save the Nation Association, with this intention in mind. However, the association has an even more important purpose, which is to practice the word "frugality." Dr. Sun Yat-sen's teachings have eight virtues: loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, trustworthiness, righteousness, peace. These eight virtues are concrete in times of national crisis. While military affairs, finance, and diplomacy are all important, the concrete foundation is still frugality. Therefore, to achieve the eight virtues of loyalty, filial piety, etc., one must start with practicing frugality. Achieving the eight virtues is not easy, but practicing frugality only requires determination. Those who are thrifty are certainly diligent. Those who are thrifty and diligent can certainly be loyal to the country, can be without contention with others, and can be sincerely united with everyone. Therefore, only frugality can save the nation. (29th, Central News Agency)

Central Party Headquarters Memorial Week

(Nanjing) The Central Party Headquarters held its 80th Memorial Week on the morning of the 29th at 8:00 AM. Attending were Ye Chucang, Ju Zheng, Wu Jingheng, Chen Lifu, Li Ciwen, Huang Jichen, Wang Luyi, Wang Faquan, Hong Ludong, Ke Xing'e, and approximately 600 staff members. Wu Jingheng presided over the ceremony, led the attendees in paying their respects, and gave a general report, stating that Japan has always been able to exploit all the weaknesses of other countries to carry out its extreme imperialist aggression. Because our country has many weaknesses, its ability to cope with the environment is insufficient, and it is bullied everywhere. The cessation of military action in the north is really just a temporary respite and should not be taken to mean that there will be no more trouble. We must seek fundamental ways to become strong. Others say that we have no organization, but in fact, our organization is complete. It is only that the people have no ideology. Originally, mass belief in an ideology begins with compulsion. Besides unconditional absolute obedience and belief, there is no need for discussion or hesitation. This principle holds true in ancient and modern times, both in China and abroad. Our country should still take the spirit of the previous Kuomintang and require the whole country to respect and absolutely believe in Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Three Principles of the People. Because Dr. Sun Yat-sen created the Republic of China, all people of the Republic should unconditionally believe in the claims of their founding father. When a nation has an ideology, it gains strength. What is there to fear about being unable to save the nation? After finishing his speech, the meeting was adjourned. (29th, Central News Agency)

Commemoration Measures for Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Enshrinement

(Nanjing) It is heard that for the Commemoration Day of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Enshrinement on June 1st, the Central Party Headquarters will still follow the commemoration measures of previous years, setting it for 8:00 AM, when all members of the Central Committee will go to the Mausoleum to pay their respects. Jiangsu Province Decides to Complete the New System of Weights and Measures in Two Phases

(Nanjing) Jiangsu Province has decided to complete the standardization of the new system of weights and measures in two phases. Thirty-five counties, including Jiangning and Jurong, will be in the first phase, scheduled to be completed by the end of June. Twenty-six counties, including Jintan and Gaochun, will be in the second phase, scheduled to be completed by the end of October. It also announced the methods for evaluating and inspecting the rewards and punishments of county magistrates for promoting the new system. Those who have completed it will be commended and credited; otherwise, they will be reprimanded and demoted. (29th, Central News Agency)

Gandhi Ends Fasting

Weak Vitality, Doctors Advise Urgent Rest

Crowds Celebrate Enthusiastically, Offer Food

National Daily, Poona, 29th: After the end of his fasting period today, Gandhi initially ingested two ounces of orange juice, and then rested peacefully. His physical condition did not seem to be as weak as the doctors had predicted. His fasting period expired at 12:15 PM today. At that time, Gandhi was lying on a small bed, covered with a white sheet, his eyes still shining, but his body was thinner than after his last fast, almost skin and bones. As he drank the orange juice, the doctors attended by his side. Gandhi then thanked the doctors for their attentive care during the fasting period, and said that he would rest quietly. As for the results of this fast, there are no comments from his friends yet.

Havas, Bombay, India, 29th: Gandhi's followers in Poona gathered in groups in a beautiful building on a small hill to celebrate the end of Gandhi's fasting. The crowds demonstrated enthusiastically, sang songs, and set off fireworks, using them to announce the news of Gandhi's end of fasting to residents throughout the city. Today is Gandhi's day of silence. Gandhi first performed silent prayer, then drank a cup of orange water offered by the untouchable caste. Villagers from distant places came one after another, competing to offer various items, especially honey, fresh fruit, and lotus flowers, to Gandhi. Gandhi then handwrote a declaration, instructing someone to read it to the public, saying that if God allowed him to fast and still maintain his life, it was because God still needed him to engage in other undertakings. Mrs. Gandhi then planted a mango tree in a flower bed near the small hill building, so as to leave a memorial for the end of Gandhi's fasting. The whole city is like on a holiday today. Gandhi's followers will hold a meeting in the afternoon to recite prayers of gratitude to God. The expert doctors treating Gandhi said that Gandhi now needs absolute rest.

US Treasury Secretary Morgan Case Intends to Resign

Backdoor Deals Give Opposition Party an Opening

President Invites Woodin for a River Cruise

To Discuss Solutions

Washington, 28th (Special Dispatch) - Friends of the US President claim that Treasury Secretary Woodin has told the President that if the President believes his remaining in office would embarrass the government, he would resign. However, the President has not yet decided whether to ask Woodin to resign. When Woodin was asked about this matter, he only replied that one should ask the President, adding that he has not yet resigned.

Washington, 28th (Special Dispatch) - Today, the US President invited Treasury Secretary Woodin for a cruise on the Potomac River. It is reported that the decision on whether Woodin will remain in office will be made before they return to Washington. Government officials indicate that the President felt uneasy after learning about the details of the Morgan Bank case, discovering that Treasury Secretary Woodin was also among those receiving special treatment from Morgan. Therefore, he specifically invited Woodin on the cruise to discuss solutions face-to-face. It is said that since the Senate Banking Committee discovered that Woodin had engaged in "backdoor deals" with Morgan, purchasing stocks at prices far below market value and reselling them for profit, Republican senators have been demanding his resignation. Although the calls for resignation have subsided slightly in the past two days, it is rumored that Democratic leaders in the Senate have agreed to take action to rectify the situation. However, those close to the President mostly deny these claims, some suggesting that the President and the Treasury Secretary will discuss stabilizing the exchange rate between the British pound and the US dollar. Others claim that Woodin does not fully agree with the President's financial plans, a hint of which was revealed when the President implemented the gold embargo a few days ago. In any case, regardless of what is discussed on the President's yacht, the Republican Party is determined to seize the opportunity to embarrass the opposition. Today, Republican senators issued a declaration demanding the dismissal of US Ambassador to Europe, Davis, stating that it is shocking that the President has not immediately dismissed Davis after uncovering the inside story. They also claimed that they would propose a detailed investigation in the House of Representatives on Monday into Davis's relationship with international bankers since he learned about international affairs in 1917. Davis previously served as Acting Secretary of State under President Wilson and was later appointed to the Financial Committee in Europe in 1919. He also served as a member of the Supreme Economic Council and the Reparations Commission. However, according to a claim, Davis still served as a trustee of a New York bank for most of this time.

Danzig General Election Results: Nazi Party Wins Big

Anti-Polish Policy Expected to End

Reuters, Danzig, 28th - The Nazi Party has won a major victory in the Danzig general election, securing 38 out of 72 seats. In other words, they won 107,619 votes out of 215,132, three times more than in 1930. The Social Democratic Party received 38,210 votes, the Center Party received 31,504 votes, the Communist Party received 14,800 votes, and others received 13,601 votes. Furthermore, the final results of the Danzig election are as follows: Nazi Party 38 seats, Social Democratic Party 13 seats, Center Party 10 seats, Communist Party 3 seats, Government Party 4 seats, Polish Party 3 seats. The Nazi Party gained 25 more seats than before. The election has passed without any disturbances.

Havas, Danzig, 29th - Now that the Nazi Party has gained power in Danzig, its actions will be closely linked to Berlin. Therefore, the future relationship between Danzig and Poland has become a problem. Some point out that Hitler has made declarations of peace, and the Polish government has also guaranteed to maintain order. Additionally, Nazi Party leader Koch has agreed to leave Danzig to avoid demonstrations, which may signal a possible easing of tensions. Polish individuals are optimistic about the failure of the National Rights Party, as it constantly opposed Poland during the election campaign. Since 1930, the Danzig Senate's policies have been anti-Polish, which has caused some disturbances. With the Nazi Party's victory, this anti-Polish policy may come to an end. The Nazi Party is well aware of the necessity of cooperation with Poland, and its published party platform does not include any attacks on Warsaw. This has reassured most residents of Danzig.

Tension in Chahar -

Feng Yuxiang Becomes Commander-in-Chief of the Anti-Japanese Army

Obstacles on the PingSui Railway

Special Dispatch from Beiping - The Japanese army is determined to seize Chahar in order to complete its so-called Manchuria-Mongolia policy, controlling China from the south and resisting Soviet Russia from the north. After the situation in Pingjin (Beiping and Tianjin) eased, the defense of Chahar Province became tense. Lieutenant General Isoya, Chief of Staff of the Kwantung Army, stated that taking Zhangjiakou is necessary to ensure the security of the Manchurian border. Military headquarters also intend to retreat to the Great Wall for future plans in the west. Recently, although the first step of the local peace negotiations within the Great Wall has been agreed upon, and the second step of resolving diplomatic issues is underway, the Japanese army has temporarily suspended the advance of troops entering the pass during this period and shifted its attention to Chahar, beginning preparations for aggression. After the traitorous troops of Liu Guitang and Cui Xingwu occupied Dolun, the Japanese army supervised their actions while transporting large quantities of military supplies to Dolun in preparation for invading Chahar. Liu and his men repeatedly telegraphed the support associations and the troops stationed in Chahar Province, stating that there was nothing unusual, but they claimed that Japanese cavalry were monitoring them and that they could not act freely until the opportune moment. As for the Chahar volunteer army and various miscellaneous troops, their organization is complex, they are not under unified command, and they lack both pay and equipment, making their combat effectiveness weak. Unless methods are devised to prepare them as soon as possible, the defense of Chahar Province is precarious. Feng Yuxiang has been living in Zhangjiakou for a long time and advocates thorough resistance against Japan. He has been in contact with various parties for two months. Since Fang Zhenwu's troops arrived in Chahar Province, he has become even more active. Yesterday (the 26th), he assumed the position of Commander-in-Chief of the People's Anti-Japanese Allied Army in Zhangjiakou. Sun Dianying and Fang Zhenwu have joined forces with him, each serving as a commander. Feng originally had a guard of several hundred men in Zhangjiakou. Recently, he recruited new soldiers and reorganized a part of the volunteer army. Since retreating from Rehe, Sun Dianying's troops have been stationed in the Chicheng area, with approximately 30,000 soldiers. Fang Zhenwu has combined his old troops, the Bao Gang and Zhang Renjie armies, and stationed them in the Xuanhua area. A few days ago, he suddenly disarmed He Sui's 2,000 troops, seized their weapons, and replenished his forces, making preparations. He now has about 20,000 soldiers. Tang Yulin's troops have automatically entered the Rehe territory, and Tang's whereabouts are unknown. The situation of Feng Zhanhai's volunteer army in the Kangbao area is also unclear. After Feng Yuxiang assumed office in Zhangjiakou, a lengthy telegraph of over 600 words was sent to Beiping today (the 27th), stating the reasons for assuming office. The main points of the telegram roughly stated, "I, as the Commander-in-Chief of the People's Anti-Japanese Allied Army, lead like-minded soldiers and civilians to form a front, armed to resist Japan and defend Chahar Province. All who genuinely resist Japan are friends of the nation and therefore my friends. All who do not resist Japan or falsely resist Japan are enemies of the nation and therefore my enemies." After Feng's telegram arrived in Beiping, it attracted considerable attention from all parties. Yesterday (the 26th) afternoon, the PingSui Railway experienced obstacles in the Xuanhua area, and traffic was temporarily interrupted. The Ping-Zhang telegrams were also blocked. Today (the 27th) at 7:00 a.m., it was fully restored. The PingSui Railway Bureau plans to establish a branch office in Datong. Duan Zonglin, the deputy director of the railway, has gone to Datong today to prepare everything. Based on the current situation, the situation in Chahar is becoming increasingly tense. If the Japanese and puppet troops invade the west, Feng and others will definitely fight to the death. Although the outcome is difficult to predict, the situation is worthy of attention. (May 27th)

He Chengjun Departs for Western Hubei to Inspect

Detailed Discussions with Xu Yuanquan on Plans to Suppress He Long's Bandits

Bandits in Eastern Hubei Fled to Southern Henan, No More Bandit Traces

Correspondence from Hankou - He Long's bandit gang, trapped in western Hubei, knowing that holding out was not a viable plan, sent out members to flee in all directions, attempting to find a way out. Apart from once fleeing to eastern Sichuan, they twice fled to western Hunan and central Hubei, but were always blocked by the strict defenses of the National Army, and eventually had to retreat back to Wufeng in a sorry state, having lost more than half of their strength. Recently, it was heard that Xu Xiangqian's bandit gang was causing trouble in northern Sichuan again, becoming active. Xu's bandits previously fled to Sichuan to provide remote support to He Long's bandits, forming a mutual defense. When Xu first entered Sichuan, he took advantage of the exploitation by warlords to incite the masses, which was very effective. Therefore, they were very active. However, Tian Songyao, concerned about his survival, worked hard to suppress them. Xu's bandits suffered repeated defeats, and hearing that the Liu-Deng war was imminent, they did not want to stay in Sichuan and prompt the Sichuan warlords to unite. Thus, they completely abandoned Bazhong, Nanjiang, and Tongjiang, and retreated to the Shaanxi border to show that they had no intention of re-entering Sichuan. In reality, they were still waiting for an opportunity. Not long after Xu's bandits left Sichuan, the Liu-Deng war unfortunately broke out. Tian only left two divisions to defend northern Sichuan, and the rest were sent back to participate in the civil war, leaving the defenses of Tongnan empty. At this time, Xu's main force had approached Hanzhong and, upon hearing the news, immediately dispatched a force back to northern Sichuan, arriving at Kushuba in Tongjiang County. They made contact with Tian Songyao's troops, and it was said that Tian's troops suffered some losses. Initially, they were guests on foreign soil, but now they were outnumbered. He Long's bandits, seeing that Xu's bandits had re-entered Sichuan, thought they would strike to provide support and planned to break out with all their strength. Their destination is still unknown, but they were likely to flee to Sichuan and form a pincer movement with Xu's bandits. He Chengjun, the Pacification Director stationed in Hubei, was ordered by Chiang Kai-shek to reside in Hankou and was responsible for overseeing the suppression of bandits in Sichuan and Hubei. Seeing that He Long's bandits were in dire straits, he planned to eradicate them in one fell swoop. To understand the bandit situation and discuss plans to suppress them with Xu Yuanquan, he took a mail plane on the 27th, braving the rain to inspect Shashi. When they reached Yuekou, the wind and rain intensified, and heavy clouds prevented them from continuing. They turned back to Hankou and rescheduled their departure for the 28th or 29th. Xu Yuanquan will issue a general suppression order as soon as He arrives in Shashi. It should not be difficult to eliminate this bandit force. The only concern is Xu's bandits on the Sichuan border. Kuang's bandits in eastern Hubei are still on the border between Henan and Hubei, and there have been no major movements recently. However, a faction from Yinghuo has split and fled through the east-west boundary ridge to the eastern countryside of Lihuang County in southern Henan. Wei Lihuang and Chen Jicheng are preparing to suppress them. Kong's bandits in southern Hubei were previously defeated by the Hunan army and fled back to the Jiangxi border. The remnants fled to the vicinity of Jinniu. According to a telegram from the commander of the 82nd Division, Rong Jingfang, they have been completely annihilated by that unit. Currently, He Jian, the commander of the western route, is launching a large-scale general offensive against this bandit force, making it difficult for them to cause trouble on the Hubei border again. Looking at the areas plagued by bandit disturbances, apart from Xu's bandits, He Long, Kuang Jixun, and Kong Hechong's three bandit forces are all within Hubei Province. Therefore, Hubei has suffered more than other provinces. The Hubei Provincial Party Headquarters specifically sent letters on the 26th to the command headquarters for suppressing bandits in the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, the Pacification Commissioner's Office, and the provincial government, requesting them to devise methods to eliminate them and secure the local area to eliminate hidden dangers. The letter stated, "The 103rd meeting of this committee passed a temporary motion to investigate the communist bandits in this province. Apart from the central Hubei area, which has been cleared, other areas have recently seen the resurgence of communist activity, and there is a risk of revival. It is proposed that this committee send letters to the command headquarters, the Pacification Commissioner's Office, and the provincial government, requesting them to devise methods to suppress them and eliminate the root cause to prevent them from spreading. It was also decided that the major bandit forces in this province were previously suppressed by Commander-in-Chief Chiang during his visit to Hubei, and they have been repeatedly routed. Only remnants remain, and the responsibility for clearing them has been assigned to various armies. We thought that these insignificant bandits would soon be completely annihilated. Unexpectedly, recent reports indicate that the remaining bandits in various counties have continued to grow. If we do not suppress them in advance, the hidden dangers will be profound. We are sending this letter to you, requesting you to devise methods to eliminate them and secure the local area." The Department of Civil Affairs and the Relief Committee, recognizing that the bandit disasters in western Hubei, northern Hubei, and eastern Hubei are the most severe, decided to allocate 77,000 yuan to provide emergency relief to the victims. On the 27th, Xie Shubin was appointed as the relief commissioner for Jun, Yun, and Yunxi counties, Dai Lizhen was appointed as the relief commissioner for the border area between Huang and Ma counties, Wang Hu was appointed as the relief commissioner for Fangxian, Baokang, and Yiju counties, and Chen Yichen was appointed as the relief commissioner for Xingshan, Badong, and Wufeng counties. They departed with the funds that day. Although it is a drop in the bucket, it is better than nothing. (May 27th)

A Visit to the Guangxi Reclamation and Water Conservancy Pilot Zone

Correspondence from Guangxi - Recently, the call for rural reconstruction has been growing louder, and the government has even established a Rural Reconstruction Committee, demonstrating the importance that the people of the country attach to this matter. However, opinions vary on how to achieve reconstruction and where to start. Most people advocate starting with relief efforts, such as improving agricultural production, providing low-interest loans, developing water conservancy, and promoting rural education. The recent resolutions of the Rural Reconstruction Committee reflect these ideas. The Shandong Rural Construction Research Institute in Zouping County, Shandong, also promotes these same goals, such as revitalizing agriculture and improving rural areas. Relief for rural construction and Zouping Village is now recognized by most people in the country as the only way to revive the countryside. Regardless of its future effectiveness, we must recognize it as a powerful theory today. Therefore, we must pay attention to and study any rural projects that are based on this theory and put into practice. I am currently residing in Guangxi and heard that there is a Guangxi Reclamation and Water Conservancy Pilot Zone located between Liuzhou and Liucheng in Guangxi. Recognizing it as a rare rural project in Guangxi Province, I made a special trip to visit it. I will now briefly describe my observations and report them to the people of the country as a reference for those who are concerned about rural issues today.

(1) Overview of the Guangxi Reclamation and Water Conservancy Pilot Zone

The pilot zone is located in central Guangxi, between Liuzhou and the Shapudongquan Shidong area in Liucheng. It covers an area of approximately 2,000 square li, extending over 100 li from Liuzhou to the north of Shapu in the north-south direction and 90 li from Liucheng to the east of Dongquan and Shidong in the east-west direction. The total area of the zone is in the shape of a rhombus. The headquarters is located in Shatang, 35 li south of Liuzhou County, and can be reached directly by car. The director of the zone is Wu Tingyang, the former Director of Construction of Guangxi. The Guangxi Provincial Government allocates 100,000 silver dollars (approximately equivalent to 70,000 Shanghai dollars) each year to fund the zone. The total population of the zone is approximately 75,000, distributed in 156 villages. Among them, those who migrated from Hunan account for 40%, those who came from Guangdong and Wuzhou account for 30%, and the rest are Zhuang people, natives of the Liuzhou and Guilin areas similar to the Yao people. This area was once occupied by Shen Hongying, and Lu Rongting also resided here. Due to years of war and numerous bandits, the local economy is extremely depleted, and the population density varies. Apart from the area near Dongquan, where the population is relatively dense, the rest of the zone is a vast wilderness with a very sparse population. A simple map is attached below.

(2) Development Process

The zone was originally part of the Liujiang Forestry and Reclamation Office. However, after five or six years of operation, it had no development due to various reasons. In March of the 21st year, it was reorganized into the Guangxi Reclamation and Water Conservancy Pilot Zone, operating independently. Therefore, the zone has only been operating for one year. However, due to careful planning and diligent implementation, the achievements in the past year have been quite remarkable. When I was in Liuzhou, I met Mr. Lie Ganzhi, who was sent to China by Harvard University in the United States to study insects. He said that he had traveled all over China for more than two years and had seen countless villages. Among the rural projects he had seen, only Beibei in Baxian County, Sichuan, and this zone were worthy of attention. He highly praised this.

(3) Zone Administration Policy

The zone's administrative policy can be summarized as transforming the old rural areas and building new rural areas. The zone believes that due to environmental constraints, the first step is to increase production so that farmers have considerable economic power. Only then can the zone demand rural self-governance from the farmers. The zone believes that the first thing to do is to ensure that every farmer has enough to eat. This is an inviolable principle. After every farmer has enough to eat, the second step is to ask how to make farmers eat better and live more comfortably. At the same time, the zone believes that everyone should have enough to eat, not just a few. Furthermore, those who work with their minds should not be able to eat well and live comfortably while those who work with their hands should eat poorly and live uncomfortably. Therefore, its consistent advocacy lies in "the tillers owning their land," realizing an equal society and eliminating the gap between the rich and the poor. The name "Reclamation and Water Conservancy Pilot Zone" is actually inconsistent with the zone's objectives. However, to avoid social misunderstanding, this name was used. In fact, the zone's purpose is not limited to reclamation.

(4) Operational Steps

The operational steps for the area will be carried out in two phases. The first phase will focus on improving rural economic organizations and implementing land reclamation policies. In addition to continuing the projects from the previous phase, the second phase will focus on various social and political facilities. These are described in detail below:

(A) Improvement of Economic Organizations: This is the first step into rural areas, and it will be carried out through three types of projects:

(1) Establishing Lending Offices: The nature of the lending offices is equivalent to that of credit cooperatives, but their content is even more comprehensive than the credit cooperatives commonly seen. First, the lending office will directly handle loans to farmers without involving village chiefs or district heads. Second, the collateral is not based on tangible assets such as farmland and houses, but on the farmer's daily creditworthiness and diligence. Third, the loans are borrowed by the area from the Guangxi Bank. The Guangxi Bank charges 1% interest, and the area also charges 1% interest when re-lending to farmers, without adding any handling fees, etc. It is entirely voluntary, so the lending office can truly serve the farmers, unlike ordinary cooperatives. The reporter asked the person in charge of the office why they did not directly use the name of "credit cooperative." The response was, "We are not yet sure whether the business we are currently running can truly meet the spirit of a credit cooperative. If it reaches a certain stage and a definite name is needed, we can hang a sign at the door that says 'Guangxi Liucheng County Tianzi No. 1 Shatang Credit Cooperative' so that the name matches the reality." Although the words were humorous, they were also said with sincerity. We looked at each other and laughed.

(2) Trial Operation of Warehouses: The most painful thing for farmers is the high interest rates charged by landlords in rural areas. This is the case in all countries. In the rural areas of Liuzhou, Guangxi, interest rates can be as high as three times the principal per year. If farmers do not have sufficient savings during lean seasons, they often resort to drinking poison to quench their thirst, willingly accepting the oppression of high interest rates without resistance. When the new grain is harvested, grain merchants manipulate and monopolize the market, deliberately suppressing prices. Farmers have no choice but to sell the grain they produced at a high cost at a low price. In addition, there are many internal customs checkpoints, making exchange difficult. In famine years, they cannot purchase grain from other places for relief, and in bumper years, they cannot sell surplus grain to places with poor harvests, resulting in falling grain prices and harming farmers. In short, whether in famine or bumper years, farmers only have one path: bankruptcy. After several years of such cycles, the average farmer is bled dry, and even self-sufficient small farmers are declining. This is the general situation in China today, and Guangxi is no exception. In view of this, the area has created a warehouse to store grain for farmers. In bumper years, it stores the surplus grain of farmers to maintain market prices, and in famine years, it distributes it to provide relief. It can also be used to provide grain during lean seasons. Its nature is different from ordinary granaries, and it is actually similar to the godowns in Shanghai. Its sole purpose is to store the surplus grain of farmers, regulate the people's food supply, and stabilize grain prices. This warehouse is closely linked to the lending office, and the method is excellent and the intention is beautiful.

(3) Establishing Public Stores: These public stores are quite similar to consumer cooperatives and purchasing cooperatives, but they are different from ordinary consumer cooperatives. They purchase goods based on demand. When a certain item is needed, they purchase it wholesale from other places. They have mutual contact with merchants in other ports and operate chain cooperative businesses.

Of the above three projects, the area will start with the first one. After the first one has been successfully implemented, the second and third will be carried out in succession. The area believes that the first step in running rural affairs should be to make the economy work and to make farmers trust the area. Only then can farmers unite and be led. These three projects are precisely the means to deeply penetrate the rural areas and establish a close relationship with the farmers. It is necessary to ensure that these three projects are well-managed before other projects can be carried out.

(B) Implementing Land Reclamation Policies: This is a plan for further building new rural areas. The barren land in the area is divided into three types: 1. Paddy fields, 2. Highlands, 3. Mountain land. The land reclamation methods are also divided into three items that are carried out simultaneously, which are described in detail below:

(1) Central Farm: This involves setting aside a small portion of land for experimentation, accounting for 300 mu in the entire area, in addition to orchards and garden areas. This experimental area can initially be freely cultivated by the settlers, but next to the settlers' cultivated area, there must be an area cultivated using scientific methods to demonstrate comparison and inspire farmers' confidence in improving farming.

(2) Economic Farm: This is a large-scale land reclamation farm, each occupying more than 10,000 mu of land and using machinery for cultivation.

(3) Cooperative Farm: This is developed by private individuals who pool their shares and receive guidance from the area.

The area stipulates that after the above-mentioned land is cultivated by the settlers, the land will be distributed to the settlers. Farming tools and livestock will be lent to the settlers at a discounted price, and the settlers will repay the discounted price to the investors in ten years. Half of the forest timber will be given to the settlers, and half will be given to the investors. The forest land will be completely owned by the settlers. At this point, the implementation of the new village can be declared complete.

The above is the work to be carried out in the first phase. After the first phase of work is completed, the work of social facilities will be proceeded with.

(Inner) Experimental School: This is the work of the second phase, scheduled to open in two years. Its purpose is to use the school as a starting point for social and political facilities, train general rural children, improve the general knowledge level of farmers, and promote the independence and autonomy of farmers.

Guangdong Communist Suppression Army Mobilizes

Eastern River troops successively advance towards Jiangxi

Southern Route Headquarters for Suppressing Bandits in Five Provinces Organized

Guangzhou dispatch: Since Chen Jitang resolved to become the Commander-in-Chief of the Southern Route for Suppressing Bandits in the five provinces of Hunan, Hubei, Guangdong, Guangxi, and Fujian, he has been actively preparing to send troops into Jiangxi to implement the second phase of the bandit suppression plan. The troop deployments are becoming increasingly active. The 1st Independent Division and the 7th and 8th Divisions of the 3rd Army in the Eastern River area have been mobilized successively. It is estimated that the two regiments of Zhong Shaokui's brigade under the 1st Independent Division and Wu Hanping's regiment stationed in Pingyuan have arrived in Dongshi, Guangdong. Ye Shiyao's regiment under Huang Zhiwen's unit of the 8th Division of the 3rd Army has moved from Xunwu to Xunbei. Xie Zheng's regiment stationed in Liuche has advanced to Xunwu, and Ouyang Xin's regiment stationed in Beiling has moved into Liuche on the Jiangxi border. Chen Feng's regiment, originally stationed in Xingning, has also been ordered to depart. The 19th and 20th regiments of Huang Yanzhen's unit of the 7th Division and Deng Hui's training regiment have also received clear orders to concentrate in Meixian and Pingyuan to prepare to enter Jiangxi. The military expenses have been discussed and finalized with the military authorities in the province by the Chief of Staff of the army, Zhou Zhi. Zhou returned to Chaozhou and Shantou yesterday to deploy everything. The labor force has been allocated by the Transportation Corps Captain to 1,700 people for distribution to various divisions. The second transportation station has been moved from Shantou to Meixian. In the future, the defenses of Chaozhou and Shantou will be taken over by Zhang Duangui's unit of the 2nd Independent Division. The defenses of Xingning will be taken over by troops sent by the 5th Division. It has been learned that the Guangdong army in the Eastern River area is focusing on the Xunwu line in eastern Jiangxi. After the Xunwu troops advance, Zhang Meixin's unit of the 4th Division in Sannan and Wang Zanbin's division of the Guangxi army will advance towards Anyuan and other places. The 1st and 2nd Divisions and the 3rd Independent Division of the 1st Army in northern Guangdong and Jiangxi will also advance towards Xingguo at the same time, with Chen Zhang's 2nd Independent Brigade remaining in the rear as a reserve force. The 3rd Independent Division stationed in Shaozhou has been ordered to begin transporting troops to Nanxiong yesterday. At the same time, more than a dozen long-distance buses have been chartered and handed over to the Nan-Shao Highway Administration for transporting military supplies. Since the Guangdong Province Communist Suppression Army has advanced on the northeast roads, it is rumored that the two-column system will be restored, with Yu Hanmou and Xiang Hanping serving as the commanders of the first and second columns, directly under the Command Headquarters of the Five Provinces Southern Route Communist Suppression. The Fifth Provinces Anti-Bandit General Headquarters is also actively being organized, and in addition to establishing one director, it is divided into staff office, military supply office, adjutant office, military law office, and political training office. The director of the executive camp may be held concurrently by Yu Hanmou, and the candidates for the heads of the various offices have also been largely determined. (24th)

Sujia Highway Nearing Completion

Road Surface Being Prepared, Expected to Open to Traffic in June

Zhenjiang Dispatch: The Sujia Highway in Jiangsu Province runs from Wuxian, passing through Wujiang, Beitan, Pingwang, Wangjiangjing, etc., to Jiaxing, Zhejiang. It is extremely important for transportation and transportation relations between Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. The road is 77.7 kilometers long. The roadbed was started in 1929, but due to funding problems, there were delays. In addition, the Shanghai War broke out suddenly last year, and part of the road project was bombed and destroyed by Japanese aircraft. Later, when Finance Minister Song Ziwen convened a highway conference in Beijing for Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui provinces, Song and others believed that this road was important and should be completed as soon as possible. According to the opinion of the National Economic Council, the original route was too remote, so the route plan was overturned, and the route below Pingwang was changed, running from Pingwang through Duanshi, Shengze, Wangjiangjing to Jiaxing. The Jiangsu Construction Department ordered the heads of the construction bureaus of Wuxian and Wujiang to remeasure, prepare a new plan and budget for approval, and then ordered them to be responsible for the project. At the same time, the Sujia Road Engineering Office was established to supervise the entire project. The road includes 48 bridges, culverts, and earthwork projects, which require time and money. The Jiangsu Construction Department originally planned to complete the entire project in March of this year, but after repeated requests for postponement from the construction bureaus of Wuxian and other places, it has recently been reported that the road bridges, culverts, and other works have been completed, and the road surface is currently being prepared. The provincial government has recently ordered to speed up the preparation, and to open the road to traffic no later than June 18. (29th)

Wuxi

Bandits Continuously Rob and Injure People

The Xunqiaotou area of Yishiyitu, Sixth District, is only two li away from the city and has convenient land and water transportation. There are three brothers, Xu Ronghua, Rongchun, and Rongkui, who are villagers there and jointly run a boat from Jiangyin Tianzhuang to Wuxi. The night before, the boat sailed from Tianzhuang to Wuxi. At around 2:00 am, when the boat passed the Xieqian Toubankou in Changjing Township, Cheng County, a bandit boat suddenly appeared. Eight or nine bandits jumped out, wearing red cloths on their heads and holding four box cannons, shouting to stop the boat. They swarmed aboard and wantonly looted, taking away goods and silver dollars worth about 300 yuan. They also stabbed the passengers with sharp blades, and Xu Ronghua was also injured by wooden objects. Afterwards, Xu Ronghua and others still sailed the boat to Wuxi and anchored. The next day, the three brothers, Xu Ronghua, etc., walked home. Unexpectedly, eight bandits came to the Xu family that night, forbidding them to make any noise, and wantonly searched and looted, causing a loss of more than 200 yuan. Ronghua and Rongkui were both shot by the bandits with pistols. After obtaining the loot, the bandits fled towards the railway from the Beizhakou area.

Tan Hongxi to Visit Wuxi Today

After a period of extreme fatigue, the local silk cocoon industry may be on the road to recovery due to the good cocoon season this year. The silkworms in the four villages have mostly ascended to the clusters. The Cocoon Industry Guild decided at a meeting on the 26th to open the cocoon weighing scale on June 1. Seventeen cocoon houses have reported to the guild that they will open. The silk factories that have been shut down in the local area are planning to resume operations. Tan Hongxi, the director of the Land Reclamation Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, will personally come to Wuxi today (30th) to understand the current situation of the local silk factories and the cocoon harvesting situation this year. He will convene a meeting with all the people in the silk and cocoon industry at the Qingye Guild to discuss everything.

Zhenjiang

Discovery of Ancient Buddha in Boyun Temple

Boyun Temple, an ancient temple in Chenwuzhuang, Zhenjiang, is more than 2,000 years old. In the third year of Qianlong, the abbot of the temple went to Tibet to pay homage to the Buddha and request scriptures. The Living Buddha bestowed three ancient steel Buddhas from the Liang Dynasty, all less than a foot high and exquisitely carved. The monk brought them back and immediately covered them with red gold, costing nearly a thousand taels. He set up a shrine to enshrine them and assigned special personnel to guard them. During the Taiping Rebellion in the Tongzhi period, part of the temple was destroyed, and the Buddhas disappeared. Later, one was discovered and sold to a temple by a certain layman for a thousand taels. The other two have not been found. It is now heard that another one has been discovered in a certain place in the southern countryside. It was unearthed by a farmer and brought to Zhenjiang for sale. The gold has been eroded, and the ancient colors are mottled. A Mr. Zhang bought it for 200 yuan and plans to send it to a temple for preservation.

The cocoon production season in the four townships of Jiaxing has largely come to an end. Fresh cocoons have already entered the market. According to a survey, only more than 20 cocoon houses have been opened in the county. The cocoon houses are very picky about the cocoons sold by the villagers. The local varieties are priced at 25-26 cents per catty at the top end, and the improved varieties are priced at 38-39 cents per catty at the top end. This year, due to the unfavorable weather, the cocoon harvest is exceptionally poor. In addition, the number of silkworm eggs raised is less than in previous years. Overall, the cocoon harvest is only 20-30%. The remaining leaves on the mulberry trees in the countryside are still eye-catching. The rural landscape can be seen here.

Lin Wojiang Talks about the Recent Work of the Aviation Association

Eighteen Fighter Jets Are Being Shipped to Shanghai One After Another

All Organizations' Fundraising for Aircraft Purchases Should Be Unified

Flying Club Can Be Established in January or February

The Chinese Aviation Association has ordered 18 Eagle brand fighter jets from the Curtiss Company in the United States. The first aircraft has been shipped to Shanghai a few days ago. The Aviation Association has scheduled to hold the naming ceremony of the Shanghai City No. 1 aircraft at Longhua Airport on June 1, and invited all sectors to participate. At that time, Colonel Du Lide, a famous American aviator, will fly the aircraft and give a public demonstration. A reporter from this newspaper interviewed Mr. Lin Wojiang, Executive Director and Secretary-General of the Aviation Association, yesterday. According to his talk, the Eagle brand fighter jet is the latest product of the United States. It has the highest speed and is extremely convenient for ascending and descending. The head is equipped with machine guns, and bombs can be placed under the ends of the two wings. It can be used as a fighter jet or a bomber, so the Aviation Association, in accordance with the intentions of the Aviation Administration, decided to order 18 aircraft and organize them into a team. The first aircraft has been shipped, and the second batch will be shipped to Shanghai in the next few weeks. As for the donations raised by the Ningbo Fellow Townsmen Association and other organizations, it is best to concentrate them. It is hoped that the aircraft styles ordered should be unified, otherwise it will be very difficult in practical command. When Mr. Lin spoke, he took the purchase of cannons for coastal defense in the late Qing Dynasty as an example. He said that at that time, various seaports ordered from England, Germany, France, and other countries. The cannons were not unfavorable, but when they were actually used, the inconsistencies in the styles of the various places resulted in the shells not matching the diameters, which delayed the war effort. It should be a lesson for us. Therefore, before ordering, all parties should have detailed consultations to achieve unification. Mr. Lin also said that the Aviation Association plans to establish a flying club first, which can be established in January or February. It is easier than establishing an aviation school. Anyone interested in aviation, after a doctor examines and certifies that they are physically qualified, pays a fee to become a member. After six months of practice, they can drive or serve in the civil aviation industry, or after several months of military training, they can be incorporated into the air defense team. The Aviation Administration has agreed to provide the Hongqiao and Longhua Airports for practice. Otherwise, huge expenses will be required to open an airport, etc.

Shanghai's First Aircraft

Naming Ceremony to Be Held at Jiangwan in Two Days

Seventeen More to Arrive in Shanghai in Stages

After Naming, to Be Donated to the Government for Inclusion in the Air Force

Central News Agency reports that the China Aviation Association, previously, due to the tense war situation, decided to first order twelve fighter planes as a gift to the government for incorporation into its squadrons for use in resisting Japan. Later, at a meeting of executive directors, it was decided to add six more planes, totaling eighteen. These were ordered from the American Aviation Corporation in batches. Some time ago, American pilot Doolittle brought the first aircraft, designated Shanghai City No. 1, to Shanghai, and performed demonstrations at the Bund and Longhua, This aircraft was purchased and delivered to Shanghai by the Association. The naming ceremony is scheduled for 2:00 PM on June 1st at the Jiangwan Racecourse. Central government officials will also be sent to attend. After the ceremony, Mr. Lin will fly the aircraft over Jiangwan for a demonstration. The remaining seventeen aircraft are said to be delivered in stages, with five expected in mid-June, ten in mid-July, and the final two in early August. After each aircraft is named, it will be donated to the government for incorporation into the Air Force. It is reported that all eighteen aircraft are of the same type, with a power of 150 horsepower. They can be equipped with machine guns and carry a large number of bombs. After delivering the aircraft to Shanghai, American pilot Doolittle originally planned to return home immediately. However, due to the need to attend the ceremony, he has postponed his departure. It is said that he will take a liner to Hong Kong in the middle of next month, and then fly to Southeast Asia before returning to Europe.

Su Zongjun and Others to Go to Hong Kong to Welcome Ma Su Back to China

Departure Changed to 2:00 PM Today

Mayor Wu Orders Preparations for Reception

Generals Ma Zhanshan and Su Bingwen, heroes of the resistance against Japan, are scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on June 5th. Su's son, Zongjun; Fan Ruizheng, the representative stationed in Peiping; Wu Huanzhang, Ma's representative stationed in Shanghai; Rong Suyu, chief of staff of Ma's forces; and Li Mingxin and others will depart for Hong Kong today to welcome them. Details are as follows:

Arrival in Shanghai in Early June

Generals Ma Zhanshan and Su Bingwen have been leading their troops in resisting Japan since the September 18th Incident. In the Nenjiang campaign, they inflicted heavy damage on the enemy. Their fierce fighting in Haimang shook the world. Eventually, on June 4th last year, due to exhaustion of ammunition and lack of reinforcements, they were forced to retreat into the Soviet Union, spending over a year in exile. They left Russia for Germany last month, and then went to Italy at the invitation of Zhang Xueliang for a meeting. On the 12th of this month, they embarked on the Italian postal ship Conte Rosso for their return to China. They are expected to arrive in Hong Kong on June 3rd, and should arrive in Shanghai on the 5th, to set foot again on the soil of their homeland, encourage their troops, and continue to resist Japan.

Heading to Hong Kong to Welcome

Besides Lang Guanpu, acting chairman of Heilongjiang Province; Jiang Songnian, a councilor; Liang Zhenduo, commander-in-chief of the Heilongjiang civilian army; Duan Zhongfan, General Ma's representative stationed in Peiping; Guo Zhutang, chief secretary of Su's troops; and others who have already gone to Hong Kong, Su's son, Zongjun; Fan Ruizheng, the representative stationed in Peiping; Wu Huanzhang, General Ma's representative stationed in Shanghai; Rong Suyu, chief of staff of Ma's forces; and Li Mingxin and others will all take the British company's Narbadala wheel to Hong Kong at 2:00 PM today to welcome Generals Ma and Su. In addition, Zhang Yan, Wang Yingjun, Shan Zhiyuan, Wang Wenkui, and other four representatives of the Northeastern people returning from Russia in Shanghai will also go to Hong Kong today to welcome them. As the two generals return to China, Xu Jingde, the acting commander of Ma's troops, is currently recuperating in Shanghai and has decided to remain in Shanghai to meet with General Ma. As for Ren Zuo, Yang Dafang, Li Yunqing, Zhan Jiazhou, the magistrate of Hulun County, Wang Weizhe, the president of the Hailaer Support Association of Heilongjiang Province, and Wang Wenying, the president of the Boketu Support Association, representatives of the Northeastern people returning from Russia in Beiping, have all arrived in Shanghai one after another and will wait for Generals Ma and Su in Shanghai.

Su's son, Zongjun, and Fan Ruizheng, the representative stationed in Peiping, visited Mayor Wu at around 10:00 AM yesterday, and then left to visit Zhu Qinglan, Chu Fucheng, and others, to thank them for their past assistance to Su's troops. Generals Ma and Su are scheduled to pass through Hong Kong without stopping and proceed to Shanghai and then Nanjing to report everything to the central government, before going to Jiangxi and Shanxi to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to seek military advice. Chairman Chiang and President Wang Jingwei are quite concerned about the safety of Generals Ma and Su, and have specifically wired Mayor Wu to make proper arrangements for their reception and protection when Generals Ma and Su pass through Shanghai. Mayor Wu has already instructed his subordinates to prepare everything.

Su's son, Zongjun, is carrying a handwritten letter from Su's father to Hong Kong, encouraging General Su to lead his old troops to make persistent efforts and continue to resist Japan, not to be arrogant in victory, nor to be discouraged in failure, to kill the enemy for the country, even unto death.

We and others will never handle a single cent to avoid suspicion, but the amount of savings should be reported to the association at any time, so that we can understand the amount of money collected in this district. Once needed, it can be concentrated immediately with just a notice from the association. In short, we and others only seek social trust and have no suspicion or worry, so that we can raise our arms and respond from all directions. The future of the country depends on this, and the long-cherished wish of the comrades will be fulfilled. At this point, everyone should embrace the spirit of fearless sacrifice. As long as we have a breath left, we cannot slack off, so as to show the true meaning and strength of the people, so that we will not be reduced to homeless people. Otherwise, it will be like the impassioned and tragic songs of the soldiers at the end of the Ming Dynasty, which are not enough to discuss saving the country. If you have any good ideas, please do not hesitate to teach us, and fight together, which is what we hope for."

China Merchants Bureau Borrows £400,000 from the Boxer Indemnity

To Purchase New Ships from England

Two River Steamers and Four Sea Vessels

Since Liu Hongsheng took over the China Merchants Bureau, he has spared no effort in reorganizing the bureau's affairs. However, because all the ships are too old to be used, a ship purchasing committee was organized to add new river and sea vessels. On the one hand, negotiations were held with the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Management Committee to borrow funds to purchase ships. This has been approved by the Ministry of Communications. Because the amount of the loan has been increased and the purchase of ships has also been slightly changed as originally agreed, it has been submitted to the ministry for approval. Yesterday, a letter was sent to the Boxer Indemnity Committee for verification. Our reporter has specially verified the general outline and recorded it as follows:

Loan Amount

Adding new ships to the China Merchants Bureau is a prerequisite that cannot be delayed. However, the required funds are huge, and the central government cannot temporarily provide this huge amount. Therefore, General Manager Liu Hongsheng was approved by Minister of Communications Zhu Jiahua to allocate a portion from the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity. Previously, it was proposed to borrow £360,000, which has been approved by Minister Zhu. Because the originally determined amount is still insufficient, General Manager Liu and Minister Zhu have agreed to increase the loan amount to £400,000, which is equivalent to approximately 6.5 million national currency at the current market price.

Purchase of New Ships

The use of the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity loan must be specified. The China Merchants Bureau will use the loan to purchase new ships. However, according to established practice, the bureau must purchase ships from England. The bureau has already agreed to this. It was originally agreed to use the funds to purchase two river steamers and four sea vessels, of which three would be regular liners and one would be a temporary liner. Now, there has been a slight change: to purchase two Yangtze River ships and four sea vessels from England, all of which will be regular liners. Yesterday, this intention was submitted to the ministry for the record.

Letter to the Boxer Indemnity Committee

Yesterday, the China Merchants Bureau sent a letter in the name of General Manager Liu to the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Committee, verifying the details of the loan amendment to £400,000 and the purchase of ships, all of which have been changed to regular liners, in order to comply with the regulations. The letter has been sent out. As soon as the committee replies, the methods for negotiating the disbursement of funds and the procedures for ordering new ships will proceed. At present, the initial procedures for borrowing funds from the Boxer Indemnity have been completed.

Grain Committee Discusses

Measures to Ban Adulteration of Rice

The Shanghai Municipal Grain Committee held its 40th regular meeting on the 26th of this month at the Bureau of Social Affairs. More than ten members attended, including Zhang Binghui, Gu Xin'yi, Zhu Zixiang, Yan Xiaoquan, Sun Yongyi, Yao Yuannuan, and Lin Dun. Chairman Zhang Binghui first reported on (1) the resolution of disputes over rice measures in the city, (2) the recent status of the original grain property division in Shanghai County, and (3) the investigation into the situation of rice merchants severely speculating. The meeting then began to discuss measures to ban the adulteration of rice. It was felt that the original punishment measures stipulated by the Bureau of Social Affairs, which stipulated that shipowners who added water to the rice on the ships would be detained and severely punished, and the original ship would be confiscated, were too severe, resulting in no one daring to report the crime. According to the rice industry association, the penalties should be reduced to: (1) If a shipowner is found to have added water to the rice, and it is confirmed to be a first offense, a fine of 55 yuan will be imposed. (2) If a shipowner has already been penalized and commits the offense again, a fine of 100 yuan will be imposed. (3) If a shipowner does not change after three offenses, the Shanghai Municipal Rice Industry Association will notify its counterparts in the interior not to engage him permanently. After discussion, it was resolved to add a fine of 100 yuan to the original third provision. The detailed measures are still to be properly drafted by the department of the Bureau of Social Affairs. Later, Committee Member Gu Xin'yi made a temporary motion to request the establishment of a method to compensate for the unfulfilled funds of the warehouse fund raising committee. It was resolved to submit the case to the Bureau of Social Affairs for review. The meeting then adjourned.

Valued at Two Million Yuan

The government is rewarding Huzhou silk exports by issuing subsidies. It has now been decided to cancel this practice starting from June 1st. Deadline June 6th
