The Barber Industry Weeps, Recounting the Gao Case

Announcement by the Shanghai Barber Industry Committee for Redressing the Grievances of the Gao Yātou Tragedy: Esteemed Sirs, we respectfully report that our colleague, Gao Yātou, also known as Gao Jinquan, was fifteen years old and the son of Gao Yuanlin from the Xiannvmiao district of Yangzhou. His father had three brothers, none of whom had sons, so Yātou served as the heir to all three branches of the family. Last August, he was introduced by Guo Wanhai to a barbershop on Rue du Père Robert in the French Concession to learn the trade. On the morning of May 7th, at 8:30 a.m., he set up a barber's stall on an open space near Qianjiatang on Avenue Albert to attract customers. Just half an hour later, a Western constable, No. 39, named Mileihong, from the Route Say Zoong Police Station came to check his permits. Gao Yātou, knowing the officer's purpose, felt for his permit but realized he had forgotten to bring it. Fearing a fine, he abandoned his barber's pole and fled north. The Western constable abandoned his vehicle and gave chase. When Gao Yātou ran to the entrance of the Wankang Sauce Garden at No. 216 Qianjiatang, he was suddenly grabbed and slapped in the face. Gao Yātou knelt down to beg for mercy but was kicked violently twice, hitting his scrotum directly. He died instantly. The Western constable, realizing the gravity of his actions, abandoned his vehicle and fled. The crowd witnessed the tragic scene and felt outraged, chasing the constable to the entrance of the Cercle Sportif Français, where they surrounded him and demanded an explanation. The Western constable went to the nearby Yangtse Bus Company to make a phone call to the police station, but was apprehended by the owner of a nearby Faji barbershop. Within moments, a large number of detectives were dispatched from the Route Say Zoong Police Station, intending to move the body and cover up the crime. The crowd prevented them and demanded that the situation be photographed and kept on file by the police station. Faced with public anger, the detectives complied. The body was taken by Tongren Fuyuantang to await examination. On May 8th, it was moved to the French Municipal Council Hospital on Route Massenet for two examinations. No family members of the deceased were present at the scene. Only Guo Wanhai, the deceased's introducer, was present during the autopsy. He described the horrific details of the abdominal incision and head sawing. However, when he inquired about the autopsy results, the doctors did not announce the cause of death. Guo Wanhai also touched the deceased's scrotum with his hand and found abnormalities, requesting that the lower body be examined together, but the doctors and officials present ignored him and told Guo Wanhai to leave immediately. However, according to news reports the following day, both autopsies found no signs of injury. Furthermore, according to reports in various newspapers on May 12th, the French police station released a statement that the investigation revealed that Gao Yātou had long suffered from lung disease, and the cause of death was heart failure due to overexertion. The results of the investigation and autopsy confirmed that running was the cause of death, and the police constable could not be held responsible. On May 10th, a general meeting of the city's barber industry was convened at the barber's guild, with representatives from the Municipal Party Department in attendance to provide guidance. A committee was formed to redress the grievances of the Gao Yātou tragedy, appealing to party and government agencies for assistance and redress. After Gao Yuanlin, the deceased's father, arrived in Shanghai, he hired a lawyer and filed a petition with the Prosecutor's Office of the Second Special District Court to request a re-examination. The petition was denied with the response that "the requested re-examination cannot be granted." The above are the details of the Gao case, tearfully reported to all sectors of society, asking for attention and upholding justice. We hope to gain serious diplomatic backing to achieve victory, to comfort the departed soul, and to uphold the rule of law, so that the nation's future will not be bullied by foreigners. We deeply believe that the power of our masses cannot be underestimated.

A separate declaration was issued, with the minimum demands being: punish the perpetrator, provide compensation, offer apologies, provide guarantees, improve police affairs, and re-examine Gao's body, among other things.

The Li Guojie Case Continued Yesterday

The Gatekeeper and Gardener of Meiliyuan Both Testified in Court

Li's Confession at the Prosecutor's Office Was Full of Contradictions

丨Today, the Westerner Sadler Testified in Court丨

The case of Li Guojie, former general manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, accused of secretly selling assets to the detriment of the company's interests and bribing Chen Fumu with 700,000 taels of silver, continued yesterday at 1 p.m. in the First Criminal Court of the Higher Court, again at the First Court of the District Court. In addition to ordering police chief Chen Junfang and police officer Chen Xihui to maintain order, Li was also transferred from the Shanghai Hospital after the case. Witness Qu Shuyou, 29 years old, from Anhui, testified.

Meiliyuan on Daxi Road

Holds the position of gatekeeper. Asked, "Do you recognize Li Guojie?" Answered, "I do not recognize him." Asked, "Do you recognize Chen Fumu?" Answered, "Yes, he is a tenant in the garden." Asked, "Does he live at No. 8?" Answered, "Yes." Asked, "Is there also a Chen Zhusheng?" Answered, "I don't know." Asked, "Does Chen Fumu have a family?" Answered, "Yes." Asked, "When did he move in?" Answered, "He moved in around November 27th or 28th last year. I don't remember the exact time, but approximately

Half a Year"

Asked, "Do you recognize this woman Wei Zhenhong? Is she Chen Fumu's wife?" Answered, "We don't know." Asked, "Do you recognize any of Chen Fumu's friends who came and went?" Answered, "I do not recognize them." Asked, "Did Li Guojie come to visit?" Answered, "I have never seen him." Asked, "Did Wang Yunzhang or Huang Jusu come?" Answered, "I don't know." Asked, "Where did he move to?" Answered, "I don't know." Asked, "Does he

Have Any Banking Relations"

Answered, "I don't know." Witness Yao Dekui, 44 years old, from Lanxi, was also brought to testify, working as a gardener at Meiliyuan. Asked, "Do you recognize Li Guojie?" Answered, "I do not recognize him." Asked, "Do you recognize Chen Fumu?" Answered, "Yes, I recognize him, he is a tenant." Asked, "Have you seen his family?" Answered, "Yes, I have seen them." Asked, "Do you know the family name of his wife and mother?" Answered, "I don't know." Asked, "When did he move in?" Answered, "He moved in in November of the 20th year and moved out in November last year." Asked, "How many people were in the family?" "Did Li Guojie Come?"

Answered, "I don't know." Asked, "Did Wang Yuanzhang or Huang Ju'an come?" Answered, "I don't know." Asked, "Who is the landlord?" Answered, "Liu Zhilu." Asked, "How much is the monthly rent?" Each Building Has a Garden"

We two are in charge, and we are already too busy, so we didn't pay attention. At this point, asked Li Guojie, "Have you been to Chen Fumu's house?" Answered, "Yes, I have been there. Chen Fumu's family lives inside No. 8." Asked, "Is it true that you wrote the letter to the Ministry of Communications?" Answered, "Yes, it is." Asked, "You said there were unavoidable difficulties, you should say them. The presence or absence of a crime, and the severity of the sentence, will be different." Answered, "Chen Fumu took away 700,000 taels, and he ran away again. Although I was ordered by my superiors, I want to prove that the money is not with me, so I wrote the letter to report it. In fact, I can say the content of the letter, but the country has many troubles, so avoid creating more complications." Asked, "What are the unavoidable difficulties that you mentioned when you said 'not hesitating to spend a small amount to achieve a big plan'?"

Answered, "I don't know if he will come." Asked, "Was giving it to Chen Fumu an individual decision or the entire board of directors?" Answered, "Neither. He is the director, and I am a subordinate. I listen to his orders in everything." Asked, "Did the board of directors know?" Answered, "I am the chairman of the board. The other directors were dismissed by the former minister Wang Boqun, and I was told to act on behalf of the board of directors." At this point, the lawyer said, "This letter was written at 3:30 p.m. on October 13th. Please note that it may not have been a free will, so Li Guojie is afraid to say it because it is of great importance." At this point, the official announced that the case has ordered Dou Yaoting to accompany Sadler to the case to testify. According to Dou, he will definitely come tomorrow. The case will continue to be heard and debated the next day, and then the court adjourned.

The Securities Departments of Two Exchanges Merge

Ending at the end of the month and merging on the first of next month

Regarding the merger of the securities departments of the Shanghai Chinese Securities Exchange and the Shanghai Material and Port Securities Exchange, both parties have decided that each will end its operations on the 31st of this month, and from June 1st, the securities department of the Material and Port Securities Exchange will be incorporated into the Shanghai Chinese Securities Exchange. All merger issues have been decided. It is understood that because the closing period is imminent, both parties have decided to convene a meeting of brokers at 4 p.m. today to discuss everything and then handle the closing and merge as scheduled.

China Chemical Industry Society

Invites All Sectors to Visit the Chrysanthemum Garden

Anyone Interested in Agricultural Production Can Participate

Pyrethrum is a medicinal plant whose properties are insecticidal. Japan and European and American countries not only use it as an important raw material for industrial societies, but also as a major agricultural product. Japan alone has an annual income of tens of millions of yuan. In order to strive for self-sufficiency in raw materials, the China Chemical Industry Society has established a pyrethrum garden in Yujidun, Shanghai. Now is the time when the pyrethrum flowers are in full bloom. In order to arouse the attention of those interested in agricultural production, the Society has specially scheduled to invite all sectors to visit tomorrow (31st). All transportation equipment will be provided by the Society. Anyone interested in visiting must prepare a letter of introduction from a group or business and register at the Society's head office at 257 Henan Road today to receive a visiting pass. Depart at 8 a.m. the next morning and return at about 11:30 a.m. It is expected that those interested in agriculture will actively participate.

The Assassination Case on Xinqiao Road

丨The Deceased, Sun Zhiwen, Was Stabbed with More Than Ten Axes丨

Originally Committed a Blood Case

Met an Untimely Death in Shanghai

Riri News reports that at around 8 a.m. yesterday morning, a vegetable-selling villager was carrying vegetables to the market when he passed by the railway next to Xinqiao Road. He suddenly saw a male corpse lying in a mud ditch beside the road, covered in blood. An axe was embedded in the head. The villager was shocked and rushed to report to the nearby police officer. They rushed to check and found that a man of about thirty years old had been assassinated. He was stabbed with more than ten axes all over his body, and the flesh was blurred. The corpse was wearing a plain white free cloth short jacket, a Zhigong twill single shirt, black rubber shoes, and a white silk belt around the waist. The police reported to the Gaochangmiao Police Station of the Second District and asked Gu Xigen, the local security officer of the 15th Tu, to report to the local court and request the prosecutor to go to inspect the corpse. It was then found that the deceased's name was Sun Zhiwen, from Gao County, Baoding Prefecture, Hebei Province. He was a weaving worker in the Yucheng Factory. He came to Shanghai with his cousin Sun Wenhua (a worker in the Hengfeng Cloth Factory), Chen Xiao Chen'er (who had returned to his hometown a few days ago), and Xiao Hei'er (unemployed and living in the Wenmeiju Restaurant on Luban Road) in January of this year and sought refuge with his fellow villager Lu Wenru (Lu is also a worker in the Yucheng Cloth Factory). Lu introduced the deceased to work in the factory. According to the deceased's cousin, the deceased had committed a blood case in his hometown, so he fled abroad. Now, unfortunately, he has been assassinated, presumably by his enemies.

Yesterday Morning, Boat Dwellers on the Suzhou Creek Petitioned the Municipal Government

The Municipal Government Approved a Three-Month Extension for Relocation

Along the Suzhou Creek in Huxi, Shanghai, there are poor boat dwellers extending for more than ten miles, totaling about a thousand people. The Second Squad of the Municipal Public Security Bureau's Water Patrol Team ordered them to relocate. These boat dwellers either work in nearby factories, carry goods at the docks along the Huangpu River and Suzhou Creek, or work as rickshaw pullers, as well as other hard laborers. If they were to relocate to distant villages, it would affect their livelihoods. Therefore, at 10 a.m. yesterday morning, they petitioned the Municipal Government. The details of the petition are recorded below:

Petition Situation

Yesterday morning, boat dwellers along the Suzhou Creek, regardless of men, women, old, or young, departed from Huxi in batches and walked to Fenglin Bridge. By 9 a.m., six or seven hundred people had arrived one after another, all gathered in the open space in front of the Municipal Government. They elected Wu Shaohua, Xia Xianyang, Cui Dengxian, Qi Guihua, and Qian Huayuan as representatives to take the petition to see the mayor. The mayor sent Xu Shaoxiu, a staff member of the Second Section, to meet the representatives. In addition to handing over the petition in person, they stated that the boat dwellers had been forced to relocate by the water patrol team, which hindered their livelihoods, and that the deadline was very tight, making it difficult to find a suitable place to make a living for a while. They requested an extension of the deadline. The chief staff member said that the instruction to relocate was due to the Junpu Bureau's dredging of the Suzhou Creek. If they were not allowed to relocate, it would hinder the dredging project. However, to show consideration for the boat dwellers, they were granted a three-month extension. If they did not relocate after that, they would be strictly dealt with. The representatives left satisfied.

Petition

In order to tearfully state the hardships and humbly request permission to extend the ban, so as to maintain the lives of the people, we poor people are unfortunate in life and lack resources, so we live by the shore and earn our living by labor. We live in small boats and have been living here for decades. Who knows that the hardships have not been eliminated, and a disaster has suddenly fallen. In recent days, the entire police of the Second Squad of the Water Patrol Team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau has been holding weapons and forcing the poor people to relocate. Those who have the slightest doubt are dealt with with iron eagle beaks, destroying the small boats where the poor people's families live. For a time, the boats leaked and sank, causing the poor people to suffer the disaster of being drowned. Those who have suffered this tragic experience are not isolated cases. Alas, we are all citizens, all with four limbs, but due to our poor circumstances, it is difficult to find a way to survive for a while, and we cannot comply with the regulations, which will lead to the doom of family destruction and death. The ancients said, "The poor have no fate." It is truly true. Rather than living to die, it is better to risk our lives to petition. We deeply hope that the distinguished seat will adhere to the Prime Minister's benevolent and compassionate purpose, strive to solve the people's livelihood, and open a compassionate heart to approve an extension of several months before imposing the ban, so as to solve the lives of more than ten thousand people. It is truly a merit.

Stop Broadcasting Siming Folk Opera

Obscene Language Endangers Social Mores and National Reputation

Ningbo Native Place Association Sends Warning to Broadcasting Station

The Ningbo Shanghai Native Place Association believes that some broadcasting stations in the city broadcast Siming folk operas with obscene language that endangers social mores. Yesterday, it sent a letter to all broadcasting stations requesting them to stop broadcasting to maintain the nation's reputation. The original letter is recorded below: The radio broadcast of various news, commercial information, music, etc., was originally intended to develop culture, facilitate commerce, and supplement social entertainment, which is a very good intention. However, recently, one or two radio stations, for the sake of profit, have adopted Siming actors' records, with obscene language, which not only endangers social mores but also affects the nation's reputation. It is indeed inconsistent with the original purpose of broadcasting. At a time when customs are declining, how can we allow fuel to be added to the fire, harming society? Therefore, this special letter is a warning. I hope you will investigate and stop broadcasting such obscene lyrics as soon as possible, so that it will be beneficial to both national reputation and social mores, and it should be pleased by your radio station.

The Chinese Medical Association Opens a Public Health Class

After opening the Physician Training Institute this spring, the Chinese Medical Association has seen many doctors from all over the country come to Shanghai for training. Most are graduates of medical schools, and the number is quite large. The training courses include internal medicine, tuberculosis, orthopedics, pathology, etc. The training locations are all in major medical institutions in Shanghai, and the talent and equipment are all top-notch. The content does not focus on lectures but on practical training, to be practical. It is reported that a public health class will also be opened during the summer vacation this year, and the curriculum has been drafted. It includes (1) the importance and scope of public health, (2) the history of medicine and public health development, (3) the management of infectious diseases, (4) vital statistics, (5) nurse and child protection, (6) school and industrial hygiene, (7) public health administration, etc. Teachers include Wu Lien-teh, director of the Seaport Quarantine Office, Li Ting-an, director of the Shanghai Health Bureau, Li Xuanguo, professor of hygiene at Tongji University, Zhang Wei, director of the Department of Hygiene at the National Shanghai Medical College, and health experts from various health research institutions in Shanghai, such as Jiang Shicheng, Wang Zhaoqi, Lai Douyan, Yu Bin, Tang Feifan, Wu Xingye, Wu Liguo, Zhang Zhisheng, and Sun Jiaqi. They all have expertise in hygiene. Gathering many experts in one place, the content is exquisite. It is generally known that the class will start on July 15, and registration starts immediately. The qualifications of trainees are limited to medical school graduates and staff of health administration agencies. The registration address is the Chinese Medical Association, No. 41 Chihbang Road, Shanghai.

Another Accomplice, the Chauffeur, is Apprehended in the Kidnapping Case of Wei Tingrong

Wei Tingrong, the former commander-in-chief of the Chinese Volunteer Corps in the French Concession, was kidnapped by bandits on Zhu Baosan Road in the French Concession at 10:30 am on July 24, 1929, and taken into hiding. The family reported the case to the French police, and after the Chinese and Western detectives rescued him from danger in the countryside of Pudong, they successively arrested three bandits, Chen Zhongheng, Tang Shiliang, and Zhu Jingcheng, and sent them to the former French Court, where they were sentenced to five years in the Western Prison. After their terms expired, they were sent to the inland authorities for interrogation. In the autumn of the 20th year of the Republic (1931), Lu Ruowang, Cai Weicai, and Zhao Weisian, three accomplices, were apprehended. The Second Special District Local Court sentenced Lu to life imprisonment and Cai to 20 years in prison. Zhao, being a military man, was ordered to be sent to the military authorities for verification. The case was concluded after three trials, and awaiting execution and transfer. On the 29th of last month, the French police discovered that the chauffeur who drove the car for the bandits at the time of the kidnapping, a local named Qian Lihe, was hiding at No. 345 Chunghua Road in the South City. They immediately went to the address, arrested Qian, and brought him back to the police station to be sent to the Second Special Court for interrogation and investigation. After the police brought back the previously convicted bandits and interrogated Zhao et al., the presiding judge of the Criminal Court, Wang Wangxu, accompanied by clerk Ren Qiyuan, came to the Criminal Court No. 1 to interrogate them. The police attorney Fei Xizhen stated the police investigation process, saying that the defendant Qian Lihe had confessed to the police that on July 24, 1929, at 7:00 am, he was invited by Zhang Adong (Zhang was murdered for adultery in September of that year) at Qinglong Bridge, Xuejiabang, to meet Cai Weicai, Tang Shiliang, etc., on the second floor of the Ping'an Hotel on Zhu Baosan Road to discuss the kidnapping of Wei. They asked him to drive the car, and he agreed to help drive the car for the kidnapping. Afterwards, Zhang told him to wait for news at No. 309 Kang Nao Road. Now the police are prosecuting him under Article 1, Paragraph 1 of the Regulations for the Punishment of Bandits. When questioned, Qian Lihe claimed to be 28 years old, formerly a chauffeur in a South City motor vehicle shop, and now unemployed. He completely denied the kidnapping case and claimed not to know Cai Weicai, Tang Shiliang, Zhang Adong, etc. The judge then ordered Cai Weicai, Zhu Jingcheng, Tang Shiliang, and Chen Zhongheng to be brought in for questioning. Cai and others were brought in in chains. When the judge asked them about the kidnapping case, they all claimed ignorance, saying that they were wrongly accused, and their answers were irrelevant. Finally, Zhao Weisian was brought in, also claiming not to know anything about the kidnapping case and not to know anyone involved. At this point, the court ordered Qian to be returned to custody and rescheduled the interrogation for June 8. Cai, Zhu, Tang, and Chen were sent back to prison, and Zhao was returned to the detention center to await instructions.

Shen Tianxi, a Victim of Economic Oppression, Commits Suicide by Poisoning

Shen Tianxi, 39 years old, from Changzhou, a plasterer who lived behind the reception room downstairs in the Qitaosheng Building, No. 9 Feixing Lane, Xinmin Road, Zhabei, made a living selling chicken and duck blood near the Gengxin Stage on Xinjiang Road. Recently, due to economic oppression, he suddenly became disillusioned with life. On the day of the Dragon Boat Festival (lunar calendar), creditors crowded his door, and in the evening, he secretly took raw opium and lay in bed, not getting up. It was not until about 2:00 pm yesterday that the second landlord, Ye Taosheng, noticed and sent him to the Pushan Hospital. The doctor found that Shen had been poisoned for a long time and could not be treated, so he died immediately. Ye immediately reported the incident to the Public Security Bureau of the Fourth District with the deceased's niece, named A Jin. The district sent police to investigate. According to Ye Taosheng, the deceased's business selling chicken and duck blood was quite prosperous, earning four or five yuan a day, but he owed too much money, and the money he earned was not enough to pay the interest. The money he borrowed was mostly usurious loans, about five or six hundred yuan, so he often said he wanted to die or not live in Shanghai, etc. He and his wife repeatedly dissuaded him, but unexpectedly last night (i.e., the night before last) he secretly took opium and died. Shen A Jin said, "I am 12 years old and the deceased's niece. I still have my biological parents in my hometown. My father's name is Shen Yansheng. I was raised by the deceased since I was a child, so he treated me as his daughter. On the Dragon Boat Festival, the deceased told me to do business well, that is, to sell chicken and duck blood, and told me to collect the money I earned. If I don't see him when I go home, I can go back to my hometown in Changzhou. At that time, the deceased still had a 'double happiness' silver coin, but now the coin is gone. I think he must have used it to buy opium. I am going back to my hometown now." After the investigating official verified the statements, he ordered Shen Xiaowu, the neighborhood head of the Eleventh Ward, to report to the Shanghai Local Court for an inquest before further verification. The body is currently kept in the morgue of Pushan Hospital.

Strictly Suppressing Flower Association Gambling

Strictly Apprehending Flower Association Kingpin Gu Malu

Flower association gambling is strictly prohibited by the police authorities of both the Chinese and foreign concessions. However, the cunning rabbits have three burrows, and they flee from one place to another. It is rare to crack down on flower association factories. Since the French

Page 10

police purchased information and cracked down on a flower association factory at No. 3 to No. 8 Fuyu Lane, Nanyang Bridge, they have strictly prohibited flower association loudspeakers and "ships" (runners) and severely punished those arrested. These people, knowing that it was difficult to gain a foothold, moved into the Chinese area and continued to operate as usual. Yesterday, they were cracked down again by the Shanghai Public Security Bureau. The details are recorded below.

Strict Suppression in the Concession

The flower association factory opened by flower association kingpin Gu Malu (nickname "Ting Luo Zi") moved from the British Concession to the French Concession. He sets up characters (numbers) wherever he goes and has no fixed place. He widely dispatches his accomplices to various roads and lanes to set up loudspeaker agencies to absorb gambling funds. In the Chinese area, he sends "ships" to collect money from house to house, and then dispatches dozens of people in cars to report characters in sections. After the French police discovered the situation, they added Chinese and French detectives to search pedestrians at the crossroads of various roads and to search houses in various lanes. They arrested and punished those who were found with flower association slips, making it impossible to set up loudspeakers and difficult for "ships" to gain a foothold. Even those who were involved in gambling did not dare to go out, and the gambling trend was greatly reduced.

The Factory Moves into the Chinese Area

At this point, flower association kingpin Gu Malu knew that it was difficult to gain a foothold in the concession, so he moved the factory to the upstairs of No. 3 Linghui Lane, Baoren Street, east of the New North Gate in the Chinese area (a "Xingji New Firm" sign was posted at the door). He continued to set up characters and receive gambling funds three times a day and night. Each character received four or five thousand gold, and gamblers flocked to it. Every time the characters were drawn, half an hour before, gamblers gathered on the sidewalks on both sides of the New North Gate.

Detectives in Disguise Arrest

The Shanghai Public Security Bureau Director Wen discovered the matter. Fearing that the information would be leaked, he secretly dispatched Hong Liang, the captain of the inspection brigade, to supervise dozens of detectives. Half of the plainclothes detectives disguised themselves as gamblers to monitor first, and then the main team of detectives rushed to arrest. As a result, they arrested 30 gamblers and seized flower association slips, account books, and loudspeakers (but flower association kingpin Gu Malu escaped). They took the people to the police brigade and immediately sent them to the Third Section of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Strictly Apprehending Flower Association Kingpin

Director Wen believes that to eradicate flower associations, it is necessary to arrest the leader and bring him to justice. Yesterday, he specifically instructed the supervisors and detective teams to strictly apprehend flower association kingpin Gu Malu and bring him to justice for severe punishment to eradicate gambling.

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Discusses Anti-Piracy Measures

In recent days, pirate attacks on merchant ships have occurred frequently. There have been multiple ships attacked, with passengers injured and crew members harmed. This not only hinders shipping but also affects travel. Liu Hongsheng, the general manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, specifically issued instructions to the heads of various departments yesterday, stating that the sea is not peaceful recently, which is very harmful to travelers and should be prevented to ensure safety. He convened a meeting of the heads of various departments this afternoon to discuss the methods of preventing pirates on sea vessels, and each presented their views for public decision. Then, he ordered the shipowners of each sea vessel to strictly comply.

The Shanghai Public Works Bureau Completes Water Transportation

The North Route is Extended to Wusong Town, Adding New Ferries

The South Route Travels to Zhoujiadu, Connecting with Automobiles

In order to complete water transportation in the entire city, the Shanghai Public Works Bureau has decided to expand the city ferry organization and add new ferries. Various plans have been carried out separately. According to Tan Boying, the chief of the Fourth Section of the bureau in charge of city ferries, to the Central News Agency reporter, the North Route facilities: The bureau currently has four large and six small ferries. Because the planned routes are insufficient, a large ferry has been added. The load and speed of the ferry are higher than the current ferries. It is expected to be completed in September and will extend the route from Tongren Wharf to Gaoqiao to Wusong Town, using the ferry to travel. The ferry terminal in Wusong Town will also be built one by one, to be realized in October. The reason why the bureau extends the route is that the residents of Wusong and nearby villages purchase goods from the shops in the 16th Pier. Not only is it inconvenient to enter and exit, but also the Shanghai-Wusong Railway does not carry cargo, relying solely on sailboats for transportation, which is a loss in terms of time and money. The citizens of Gaoqiao and Wusong are all citizens of the city and should enjoy the same convenience. Therefore, all preparations are being actively made.

South Route Plan: Water transportation on the North Route of the city will be completed after the Wusong line ferry is realized. Then, the South Route will be considered. The plan is to open one shift per hour from Tongren Wharf to Zhoujiadu to facilitate the citizens of the area. After negotiating with the long-distance company in the area and preparing the method, preparations can be made to complete water transportation in the city as soon as possible. As for the management of wharves and other affairs by the bureau, according to Shi Konghuai, the director of the wharf management office, after the bureau managed the wharf, it tried its best to eliminate various malpractices on the wharf to ensure the safety of travelers and implemented it long ago. Now it still adheres to this spirit to make the wharf management more perfect.

The Industrial Safety Association Seeks Members

The First Phase Ends on the 10th of Next Month

After the Shanghai Family Industry Society, Kangyuan Canning Factory, Yonghe Industrial Company, Tianchu MSG Factory, Tianyuan Electrochemical Factory, Chichang New Rubber Factory, and others initiated the organization of the Industrial Safety Association, they actively carried out preparations to establish it as soon as possible and began to solicit members. The announcement is as follows: In order to ensure the safety of factories, the association has joined with various factories to organize the Industrial Safety Association to jointly study methods for preventing disasters and to plan factories that prevent industrial disasters for various factories, or academic groups that support the purpose of the association, are requested to join the association as group members. All individuals or academic experts who support the purpose of the association and are willing to cooperate in promoting industrial safety are requested to join the association as individual members, so that they can work together to protect the lives and health of workers and reduce accidental losses in factories. Society and the country will be fortunate. The association plans to first solicit members during the preparation period. All those who wish to join the association are requested to fill out a membership application form (the introduction section can be temporarily left blank after the attachment). After filling it out, please send it to the association at No. 1 Jiyi Lane, Bubo Road. The first application period ends on June 10. The representatives of all group members are requested to indicate their age and position in the group.

A Foreigner's Car Runs Over a Rural Child

Shunxiang, the grandson of Ma Fusheng, a farmer in Guqiao, was walking on the Shanghai-Minhang Road near the Beiqiao County Government at about 4:00 pm the day before yesterday. Suddenly, a foreigner drove his own car at high speed, and the child was unable to avoid it, causing him to be knocked down and seriously injured by the car. The police arrived, recorded the car number, and sent the injured child to a Shanghai hospital for treatment. However, he died yesterday afternoon due to severe injuries. It was immediately reported to the court for inspection and verification.

The Actor Chen Xiaomu is Extremely Licentious

His Wife Petitions for Mediation and Divorce

Chen Xiaomu, who currently plays the old man in the Sanxing Stage, has always liked women. Since marrying Wang Naizhen in 1926 through a matchmaker, he has not known how to cherish himself and has been pursuing women and creating a bad reputation. Later, he was hired to perform in Hanzhou and dared to seduce women during the performance, which was not tolerated by the local people who attacked him and drove him away. Chen was not tolerated in Hanzhou and returned to Shanghai in disgrace. Unexpectedly, he relapsed not long after. His wife, Wang Naizhen, feared that he would repeat the mistakes he made in Hanzhou and advised him, but Chen not only did not change, but also became worse and vented his anger on her. From then on, he regarded Wang as a thorn in his side and abused her, and invited his concubine to his home to sleep with her publicly and forced Wang to wash clothes for the concubine, which was extremely tyrannical and spread scandalous rumors. Wang, because her concubine usurped her position, treated her as a servant, and was unwilling to endure her breath, naturally resisted and was beaten and kicked by Chen until September last year, when Chen even staged the "Wang Youdao Divorces His Wife" play in his home and forced Wang to leave. Wang could no longer bear it and hired a lawyer to negotiate with him. As a result of the negotiation, Chen promised (1) not to abuse her again, (2) not to seduce women again, and (3) to pay 20 yuan a month for pocket money. Therefore, they reconciled, and Wang lived with him again. Unexpectedly, Chen was fickle, the ink on the contract was not dry, and the evil thoughts of lust re-emerged. In addition to sleeping with prostitutes, he also operated a "golden house" in the Tongshan Lane on Bishi Road in the French Concession, treating his legal wife as a stranger and abandoning her. Wang negotiated with him again, but Chen was cunning and immediately moved his concubine to another place, and the house he rented in Tongshan Lane was also handed over to others. However, he stubbornly denied it after the reconciliation, but Wang felt that Chen did not fulfill his obligation to live together, was not worthy of the name of husband and wife, and continued to oppress her, making her feel unbearable. If she did not cut off the vines, her lifelong happiness would be sacrificed forever. Therefore, she decided to hire lawyer Wang Peiyuan to file a petition with the Civil Mediation Office of the First Special District Local Court, requesting that Chen Xiaomu be ordered to come to the court to mediate the divorce and to pay 30,000 yuan for alimony. This morning at 9:00, it was the date for the court to mediate, but Chen Xiaomu refused to appear, and Wang Naizhen came to the court with her representative lawyer, waiting for a long time. Because one party evaded, mediation could not be carried out, so their divorce entanglement will probably have to wait for a formal lawsuit before a ruling can be made.

Singing Girl Zhao Peiying Accuses Li Shiquan of Enticement

Zhao is the Adopted Daughter of Fan Shaoshan

Li is a Descendant of Li Hongzhang

Li Shiquan, a descendant of the former Qing Prime Minister Li Hongzhang, who currently resides at No. 4 Chongqing Road, is 24 years old. Recently, Zhao Peiying, 23 years old, the adopted daughter of Fan Shaoshan, who is famous for singing "Tan Huang," filed a complaint with the First Court of the Special District, accusing him of enticement. Yesterday was the date for the trial, which was publicly heard by Judge Wu Zelin in the Criminal Court No. 3. First, the plaintiff said that she was from Pudong and was adopted by Fan Shaoshan as his adopted daughter at the age of twelve and followed him in singing. In 1928, she met the defendant, and the two fell in love. In November of that year, they had a relationship in the East Asia Hotel. Then, he ordered her to leave the Fan family and rented a house in Yanji Lane, Garbage Bridge, and then moved to No. 46 Yongji Lane, Weihaiwei Road. At that time, Zhao was only 21 years old. In addition to paying the rent by Li, she also received 250 yuan per month for living expenses. When they had a relationship, Zhao wanted to hold a formal wedding, but Li said that the wedding was only a formality and could not be relied on, so they could take a photo together as a souvenir. Since March of this year (Gregorian calendar), the supply and Li himself have been cut off. Now, because he abandoned her after seducing her, she requests that he be sentenced according to the law and ordered to continue to bear 250 yuan per month for living expenses for ten years, requesting a one-time payment of 30,000 yuan. When questioned, the defendant Li Shiquan claimed that he completely denied the facts stated by the plaintiff. He had a friendly relationship with Zhao Peiying, but only because he was studying at school at the time and had nothing to do after class, so he accompanied friends to cheer her up. He once sent someone to borrow money because Zhao was pregnant and gave birth, with 2,500 yuan as a break-up fee, which can be proved and has an intermediary, Wu Yixiang, to testify. He married a wife the year before last and was also engaged when he met Zhao. Now he denies all the 30,000 yuan requested by the plaintiff. At this point, Judge Wu summoned the witness Wu Yiqing for questioning and ordered the lawyers for both parties to begin their arguments. After the arguments by the plaintiff's agent, Zhan Jifeng, and the defendant's agent, E Sen, the court ordered that the judgment be announced at 2:00 pm on the 5th of next month.

Huang Ziqiang is Sent to the Shanghai Public Security Bureau

Huang Ziqiang, also known as Mu Yan, is from Chengdu, Sichuan. He is 35 years old and resides at No. 25 Xingye Lane, Xiafei Road, French Concession. His brother, Huang Ying, is currently the commander of the Second Division of the 28th Army in Sichuan. Huang once served as the chief of staff of the division headquarters and is currently the Shanghai representative of Deng Hou, the commander of the 28th Army. Recently, the Shanghai Public Security Bureau received an order from the Ministry of Military Affairs and the Headquarters Garrison Command stating that Huang had reactionary communist activities in Shanghai and should be immediately arrested and sent to Beijing for interrogation. Director Wen Hongen, upon receiving the order, prepared a document and sent personnel to the French police on the afternoon of the 17th of this month to request assistance in the arrest. The Minister of Political Affairs sent Chinese and Western detectives to rush to Huang's residence at 10:30 pm that night, arrested Huang, and seized books, documents, and other evidence, and brought them back to the police station. The next day, he was sent to the Third Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court and prosecuted for endangering the Republic of China under Article 1, Section 3. After being detained for investigation, the court rescheduled the hearing. After the police completed the investigation, Zhou Yunhui, the presiding judge of the Criminal Court, together with judges Guo Dezhang and Fan Peien, and Chief Prosecutor Zhao Shibei, came to the Criminal Court No. 3 to interrogate him. The police lawyer Yuan Jiahong appeared in court, and the defendant Huang Ziqiang hired lawyer Tan Yigong to defend him. Jiang Yuewu, the supervisor of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau, along with detectives, came to the court and requested permission to transfer the defendant to the bureau for interrogation. The court then announced that because the case was related to politics, bystanders were prohibited from attending the hearing. According to reports, the court ruled that because the defendant was an active-duty military officer, the court had no jurisdiction and ordered the defendant Huang Ziqiang to be handed over to the Shanghai Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

A Counterfeit Money Headquarters is Cracked Down in Zilaishui Street

The Main Criminal, Zhou, is on the Run

Recently, there has been a group of extremely idle people who specialize in using counterfeit money in various cigarette and paper shops in the concession. However, the headquarters of the counterfeit money often moves, so it is difficult for the authorities to crack down on it. A Shandong native, Zhu Lingheng, used a ten-yuan counterfeit banknote at a small cigarette and paper shop opened by Wang Cai, a woman on Xihuade Road. Wang was unable to detect the authenticity, and sent an apprentice to inspect nearby shops. Zhu became nervous and wanted to retrieve the counterfeit banknote, causing a dispute. The Chinese detective Zhang Guisheng found out the situation, questioned him, and sent Zhu and the counterfeit banknote to the First Special District Local Court for detention. After Zhang detected that there was another accomplice, Tang Jinfu from Zhenjiang, hiding at No. 840 Fangbang Road in the Chinese area, he reported to the head of the police, and together with the Western detective, rushed to the Public Security Bureau in charge and arrested Tang, seized a bundle of white paper for printing counterfeit banknotes. He learned that the headquarters was located at No. 160 Lianmeng Lane, Zilaishui Street, French Concession, and the main criminal was surnamed Zhou. The detectives went to the French police to assist in the arrest, but Zhou had already fled when he heard the news. Only two five-yuan counterfeit banknotes and 100 bullets and a pair of handcuffs were seized. However, the prohibited items were not related to the counterfeit money case and were taken back by the French detectives for investigation. Yesterday, Tang was sent to the Special Court, and Judge Wu Zehan interrogated him. The police lawyer Chen Ming explained the situation and requested detention and presented the counterfeit banknotes for inspection. Judge Wu briefly questioned the defendant, ordered him to be returned to custody, and rescheduled the hearing to be combined with the case.

Fang Jiaobo Sends a Letter to the Fisheries Association

Liu Tonghua and other four families of the Shanghai Ice Fresh Fish Industry Association resisted paying the fishery construction fee. The Fisheries Improvement Committee issued strict orders to supervise them separately. The other day, Liu and others submitted a document stating that Fang Jiaobo, a member of the industry director and the association, had guided them. Yesterday, Fang Jiaobo sent a special letter to the Fisheries Improvement Association, the original letter is as follows: Dear Sir, I recently read a report stating that Liu Tonghua and others of the Dacheng Fish Industry Association stated in their document to your association that the association was guided by me and elected Dai Qiu and other four people to consult with the collection office and request that the method be changed and the collection be made on-site from the fishermen, and our association in Shanghai will not be responsible for withholding it. I am deeply shocked. When the association held a meeting on the construction fee, I attended and advocated that since there were many people, it was inconvenient to talk, and Dai Qiu should be elected to make an appointment with the collection office to discuss a proper method, and there was no indication that the collection should be made on-site from the fishermen or that the fish industry association would not be responsible for withholding it. What the Dacheng Industry Association said is completely inconsistent with the facts. I am afraid that there will be misunderstandings. I am writing this letter to clarify the situation, I hope you will take note of it. To the Fisheries Improvement Committee of the Jiangzhe District of the Ministry of Industry, Fang Jiaobo, May 29.

Letters to the Editor

Dear Editor, I have read the article in your newspaper that He Fangpu has not yet been released. The article states that according to investigations, although He has no master-servant relationship with Mitsui now, He's original position is still inherited by He's eldest son, so it cannot be said that there is no relationship at all. Also, it is said that every time goods arrive, He must take the opportunity to purchase Japanese sugar in bulk and obtain huge profits, which is shocking. It is found that my father was arrested by the Zhejiang Provincial authorities this time because of false accusations by those who held grudges. Once the matter is clarified, the truth will come out. However, the claim that my father's position at Mitsui was inherited by his eldest son is inaccurate. Although Bo Yan also worked at the company when my father was at Mitsui, after my father resigned, he completed the unfinished procedures and also left the relationship with Mitsui. He is now employed at Lida Zhuzhou Bearing Company, No. 81 Xihua Road in this city. The facts are all there and cannot be falsified. As for the bulk purchase of Japanese sugar, it is even more of a fabrication out of thin air. I am afraid that it will confuse the public. Therefore, I am specially writing to your newspaper to correct it in order to clarify the truth. I would be grateful. Respectfully, Shenbao Newspaper Editorial Department, Editor-in-chief, He Boyan, May 29.

Dear Editor, I have just read the news in the "City News" column of your newspaper on May 28 about the donation for aircraft purchase, which involves our factory. It is found that the aircraft donated exclusively by our factory has already been ordered and the price is above 100,000 yuan. It will arrive soon. Regarding the self-ordering and the type of aircraft purchased, the consent and instructions of all relevant parties have been obtained. The statement that "the Aviation Patriotic Association has repeatedly requested it without success, and negotiations are still underway" is completely untrue. Please correct it in order to clarify the truth. Sincerely, Shenbao Newspaper, Tianchu Monosodium Glutamate Company Manufacturing Plant Management Office, May 28.

Reader Consultant

Where to Go is the Road to Survival

丨Letter from Mr. Wang Bin of Songjiang丨

I am several years old this year. When I really have no way to go, I specially write a letter to describe my situation. Because in my childhood, I never suffered the pain of receiving a proper education. Moreover, I lost my mother one after the other before I was even ten years old. At that time, I lived with my brother. When I was fifteen years old, an acquaintance of my father from Japan introduced me to work as an apprentice in a factory. After three years, the factory director paid me a monthly salary of four yuan. It has been nine years this year. In the past, when I was a child, I could pass the time unknowingly. Now, there is no way to go. Why? It is because two years ago, my brother thought that I was of age and should establish a family. At that time, I didn't know what the heavy burden of family responsibility was, so I followed orders. Who knew that after only three years, I am already heavily in debt. Moreover, a small child was added last year. Now, the expenses have increased. Before my wife gave birth, she could still do some work to help. Now, she can't. My brother also has the burden of a family. I have exhausted my loans from relatives and friends. I want to find a job with a higher position and a higher salary. I have already said above that I have not received a proper education. I have no qualifications at all. Even if people want to hire staff, they always want people with proper qualifications. Moreover, the society is now in a panic. There are many unemployed people. There are also many people with educational degrees. Who would want to hire me? I want to improve my situation in this factory to meet the family expenses, but I can't. Because the business is now declining terribly. The boss's principle is to reduce expenses. My monthly salary is only eight yuan. May I ask how my family of several people can live now? If I ask the boss for a raise, he will immediately fire me. I am about to lose my job. I want to find work, but no one will introduce me. I want to go to the countryside to farm, but I have no land. I want to commit suicide, but I can't. Under these thoughts, I really have no way to go. I can only beg the reporter, who has insight and a virtue of loving life, to think of a perfect way to survive for me and reply!

Answer: Almost half of our readers are asking questions because they have no way out of life. This shows the widespread economic bankruptcy in the current society, not only in the countryside but also in the cities. It is really difficult for us to come up with ways for everyone to live, because this is a social problem as a whole. I hope that our dear readers, when it comes to this kind of problem, never focus only on themselves and their families, and the purpose of their struggle should not be limited to the interests of themselves and their families. Your problem is the same. I hope you think from a big picture perspective and fight for the community. A way to survive will naturally appear. Correction Yesterday's column, line 41, after "or the interests of a few people?", the sentence "or from the social interests of the majority of the masses?" was omitted; in line 53, after the three words "or Pu", the word "bian" was omitted; in line 86, the three words "with its saying" were redundant; in the second to last line, the word "the" in "the holy scripture" was redundant. Combined corrections. Communication procedures: (1) Provide full name, age, gender, place of origin, occupation, and detailed address. (2) Attach sufficient return postage. (3) Affix the communication stamp in the upper corner of this column. The description of facts in the letter should be simple and clear, and the handwriting should be clear. All letters that do not include sufficient return postage or do not provide a detailed address, except for those that may be published in this column, will not be replied to.

Education News

Important News

Students from Unregistered and Closed Private

Vocational Schools to

Take Verification Exams on a Scheduled Date

To be Held on July 15

丨The municipal department will announce after the Ministry's order arrives丨

(Nanjing, 29th) The Ministry of Education has re-promulgated the 13-article verification examination regulations for graduates and students of unregistered and closed private vocational schools and above, as well as the regulations for the examination committee. The registration date is determined by each province and city, with June 30 as the deadline. The test locations are divided into four places: Shanghai, Beiping, Guangzhou, and Wuchang. The test period is scheduled for July 15, and all four places will hold the test at the same time.

It was reported the other day that the Ministry of Education will instruct the municipal education bureau to hold another screening test and entrance examination for graduates of unregistered secondary schools and universities. Many people have inquired about this news from the municipal education bureau in recent days. The bureau has not yet received an official document from the Ministry of Education (so it is not convenient to handle it. Once the Ministry of Education's instructions are received, it will be announced and known, it said.

Guangdong Province Reforms The School System Plan is Tacitly Withdrawn

(Nanjing, 29th) The Southwest Education Reform Committee resolved to reform the school system. Previously, the Ministry of Education asked the Executive Yuan to forward the order to the Guangdong Provincial Government, which refused to implement it. After the order was issued, the Guangdong Provincial Government presented a reply to the Executive Yuan yesterday, saying that it had not been informed by the committee and could not handle it, which seems that the plan has been tacitly rejected.

Northwestern Agricultural and Forestry College to be Established in Wugong

(Nanjing, 29th) The preparatory committee of Northwestern Agricultural and Forestry College previously resolved to establish the school in Xianyang. The Ministry of Education dispatched German agricultural and forestry expert, Section Chief Fintzel, and Qiu Changgeng to Shaanxi for inspection. Qiu and others returned to Nanjing on the 29th and stated that Wugong County, west of Xianyang, is even better than Xianyang. There is an intention to relocate the agricultural college to Wugong, but it still awaits the decision of the preparatory committee.

Shandong Provincial Examination to be Held on June 1st

(Jinan, 29th) This province's graduation examination for the current academic year is scheduled to be held on the 1st. The chief examiners for each district have already departed today.

Local News

Municipal Health Exhibition - Participating Schools May Appoint Their Own Receptionists

Schools are also instructed to send staff to attend lectures.

The Municipal Education Bureau issued an instruction yesterday to primary and secondary schools and kindergartens, stating: "The Health Education Exhibition has been fully prepared and will open on June 1st. All participating schools may appoint their own receptionists during the exhibition period. They should wear badges with the school seal and provide services at the venue. Furthermore, the Health Education Exhibition will host lectures on health education methods from 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM on June 2nd. All schools with four or more classrooms should send three teachers and staff members to attend the lectures. On June 3rd, from 1:00 PM to 3:00 PM, there will be a lecture on children's healthy habits. All schools should send teachers and staff to lead children to attend the lecture to enhance their health knowledge. You are hereby ordered to comply with this instruction."

Joint Appeal from Shanghai University Students to All Students in Shanghai

The Way to Save the Nation Lies in Long-Term, Effective Struggle

Those indulging in romantic pastimes should abandon their bad habits.

Those chasing after movies and dances should eliminate their addictions.

Study "The Last Lesson" with the spirit of killing the enemy on horseback.

The Shanghai University Student Union issued an appeal to all students in Shanghai, stating: "China's internal and external troubles have reached their peak. At this critical juncture, everyone should have the spirit of passionate endeavor, indignation, and desperate effort. However, the way to save the nation lies in effective struggle, and everyone must do their best and fulfill their responsibilities. Our current responsibility as students is to study. We should deeply understand the difficulties of the current situation and always take saving the nation and revitalizing the nation as our own responsibility. Those indulging in romantic pastimes should abandon their bad habits, and those chasing after movies and dances should eliminate their addictions. With the spirit of killing the enemy on horseback, we should strive to learn, train our minds and bodies, and strengthen our will. We should strive for practicality in our studies and practice in our actions, so that we can acquire real knowledge today and shoulder the great responsibility of revitalizing the nation in the future. This is what we university students should encourage and pledge to ourselves during this period of national crisis. Recently, reactionary factions and traitors in this city have spread rumors that our students will go on strike. We sincerely do not know on what basis they say so. We recognize the seriousness of the current environment and believe that only persistent struggle can save the country. However, to engage in long-term and effective struggle, we must rely on the basic knowledge of saving the country. Shanghai students should have the spirit to finish reading 'The Last Lesson.' The model of Turkish revival is already there, and the precedent of Alsace-Lorraine is not far away. May all university students in Shanghai encourage each other."

Primary School Curriculum Compilation, Kindergarten and Hygiene Groups Complete Drafts

The various groups of the Municipal Education Bureau's Kindergarten and Primary School Curriculum Compilation Committee previously agreed to complete all drafts by the end of May. It is now reported that, in addition to the English and Arithmetic groups having already completed their work, the Kindergarten Group and the Hygiene Group have also completed their drafts and are being sent to experts for review.

Various Private Secondary Schools Hold Calligraphy Competition

Scheduled for June 18th

丨Preparing for a Joint Secondary School Library丨

Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, various private secondary schools in this city held the first preparatory meeting for the calligraphy competition at Shanghai Girls' High School. Ci Hang Wang Xuequan, Wu Zhiqian of Shanghai Girls' High School, Xu Zexiang of Tiehua, Ma Jiazhen of Huadong, and Xu Zeyi of Fudan Experimental High School attended. Wu Zhiqian chaired the meeting, and Xu Zexiang served as the recorder. The following resolutions were made: (1) Regarding the proposal to determine the date and location of the competition, it was resolved to hold it at 1:00 PM on June 18th, with the location tentatively set at Shanghai Girls' High School. (2) Regarding the proposal to send circulars to students of various private secondary schools to participate, it was resolved to be handled by Shanghai Girls' High School. (3) Regarding the proposal to determine the registration date and location, it was resolved that registration would be open from today until June 15th, with the registration location at Shanghai Girls' High School. (4) Regarding the proposal to determine the matters needing attention for each school to select competition representatives, it was resolved that: 1. Only currently enrolled students of each school are eligible to participate in the competition. 2. Each school should select two representatives. 3. The selection method should be determined by each school. (5) Regarding the proposal to determine the types of calligraphy, it was resolved to divide them into three types: regular script, small regular script, and running script. (6) Regarding how to solicit prizes, it was resolved to send letters to party and government agencies, famous calligraphers, and cultural organizations to solicit them. The distribution of prizes will be divided into group and individual awards.

In addition, the preparatory committee for the establishment of a joint library for secondary schools held a meeting yesterday. Wu Baojin chaired the meeting, and Chen Shizhong served as the recorder. It was resolved to set the budget at 100,000 yuan temporarily, raise funds, hold various technical competitions, solicit books and equipment from the national publishing industry, and request designated subsidies from the Ministry of Education and the Municipal Education Bureau. It was also decided to request assistance from the Chinese Ratepayers' Association and the concession authorities, and to invite Pan Gongzhan to serve as the honorary president.

Establishment of Chenguang Vocational School

The Chenguang Vocational School in this city, organized by university professors Hu Yaomei and others in the education field, has been approved for establishment by Municipal Education Bureau Directive No. 7824. It is reported that the school is actively engaged in preparations and will initially offer three departments: Commerce, Civil Engineering, and Applied Chemistry (divided into higher and lower levels). Enrollment will begin during the summer vacation. The founders of the school recognized that many middle school graduates are unable to continue their studies at universities due to financial constraints. They lack specialized skills and do not meet the needs of society, making it difficult for them to find employment. The school's board of directors includes Zhao Jinqing, Fu Rulin, Shi Daosheng, Liang Shichun, Xue Jimin, Cheng Xiangzhi, Hu Hanrui, Lu Jiesun, and Hu Yaomei, most of whom are prominent figures in the industrial and commercial sectors.

Chenxi Wins Two First Prizes in Music Competition

Since Principal Xuan took over Chenxi Girls' Middle School on Luban Road, school affairs have flourished. Organizations such as the student self-government association, basketball club, volleyball club, speech contest, and music association have been established. In the recent city-wide children's broadcasting competition, Zhou Yanhua and Yin Huimin, both students of the affiliated primary school of Chenxi Girls' Middle School, won two first prizes. They are only ten years old and hold the leading position in the city's music scene. In addition to receiving flower baskets and gifts from various businesses, Mayor Wu personally presented them with silver tripods and silver cups. The school also won many other prizes, such as silver cups.

Daozhong Girls' Middle School Invites Xu Zexiang to Give a Lecture

Since Principal Cui Junwu founded Daozhong Girls' Middle School at the intersection of Avenue Road and Carter Road in this city, the school's achievements have been remarkable. The school invites famous people to give academic lectures every Monday. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, Xu Zexiang was specially invited to the school to give a lecture entitled "The Outlook on Life that Modern Chinese Women Should Have." Mr. Xu's speech was eloquent and his theory was grand and abundant. More than a hundred students in the audience were deeply moved.

Zhejiang Provincial Games Day 3: Men's and Women's Track and Field Championships Concluded

Numerous New Records, 17 Men's and 5 Women's Events

Almost All Previous Zhejiang Provincial Records Broken

Zhejiang Province's Sports Have Been Progressing in Recent Years

Swimming and Ball Games Competitions Begin Today

Yesterday was the final day of track and field events for all groups at the 3rd Zhejiang Provincial Games. The weather was very good, and the number of spectators increased significantly, giving the venue a vibrant atmosphere. Overall, although the results cannot be compared with top athletes, they are much better than before in Zhejiang Province, showing significant progress. Almost all previous Zhejiang provincial records were broken. New Zhejiang provincial records were set in as many as 17 men's events and 5 women's events. Moreover, many athletes broke previous records in each event, indicating that Zhejiang Province's sports have been progressing significantly in recent years. Qi Huaizhi, Leng Peiji, Wang He, Yuan He, and others are all promising talents. The championship titles for each group have been announced. The men's high school track and field and the men's junior high school track and field championships both belong to District 1. The men's junior high school District 2 is also very close to District 1. The women's high school group was almost entirely dominated by District 1, but the women's junior high school group had many talents in District 2, overwhelming District 1 and winning the championship. The Talent-Rich 19th Route Army Soccer Team Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday

Led by Jin Yiting, Huang Meishun and 19 others arrive first

Xu Xiang and Liu Zukan from Shanghai will join the team to work together

The team will stay in Shanghai for two weeks to await the return of the East China team

The soccer team of the Youth Military Service Corps of the First Column of the 19th Route Army, led by Corps Leader Jin Yiting, arrived in Shanghai yesterday on the Jinan steamer from Xiamen and stayed at No. 4 Yipinxiang. Xu Heng and Liu Zukan from Shanghai will join the team. The team will stay in Shanghai for two weeks to await the return of the Donghua team from the Philippines for a match, before leaving Shanghai for Wuhan.

Origin of the Organization

After the 19th Route Army decided to go north from northern Guangdong, Zhang Yan, commander of the First Column, considering that many young people would enthusiastically participate in this departure, initiated the organization of the Youth Military Service Corps. In addition to setting up propaganda and other departments, there was also a sports department. In addition to sports propaganda, it could also supplement military needs with ticket income, which led to the creation of the 19th Route Army soccer team.

Members Arriving in Shanghai

The first batch of 19 people arriving in Shanghai yesterday included Corps Leader Jin Yiting, Section Chief Chao Zhongyuan, Secretary Wu Qinrao, and team members Huang Mei , Tang Kun, Zheng Shaokang, Liang Darong, Du Kecheng, Yang Benhan, Yang Guohua, You Huaxing, Gan Xihui, Xu Yaoxian, Hui Lin, He Qi, Zeng Zhi , Tang Baoxing, Huang Xing, Lin Dacheng, Zhang Xiuquan, Zhang Shao . Many of them are soccer players from Sun Yat-sen University in Guangzhou.

Second Batch Arriving

The four knights of the South China Soccer Team, Feng Zuixiang, Tan Liangbai, Bei Hua, Li Tiansheng, as well as Zhu Guolun, Jiang Zan, Huang Jiliang, and Huang Dingfen, will come in the second batch. The date of their arrival in Shanghai is currently uncertain. The players from Shanghai who will participate are Liu Zukan and Xu Heng.

Activities in Shanghai

The team will stay in Shanghai for about two weeks. Now is the end of the soccer season. The West Union team no longer exists, and the Donghua team has also gone south to the Philippines. The Shanghai Football Association and Yu Heng are in contact to arrange matches in Shanghai. They will probably play several matches. The Donghua team is expected to return to Shanghai around June 12th. The team will wait for their return to Shanghai and will also arrange a match. The issue of the venue is being discussed with Shen Siliang.

Leaving Shanghai for Wuhan

After the match with the Donghua team, the team will leave Shanghai for Hankou around the 15th to join the army. They will then leave Wuhan for the north. There will also be one or two matches in Wuhan. The issue of going north cannot be predicted at this time.
