Spring and Autumn

Breaking the Mystery of the Current Situation

— Shan Lu

Is the mystery of the current situation not easy to break? Easy, easy.

What way to break the mystery of the current situation? Break it two ways, by reversed riddle and by tying a bell with a red bean.

Those who love riddles will certainly understand the way to guess them. There is the reversed riddle, to read the riddle backwards. There is the bell-tied riddle, to add a voiceless word to the riddle. There is the red bean riddle, to make one sentence of the riddle into two sentences. Whatever negative words, by using a reversed riddle can be changed into doubt and uncertainty. By using a bell-tied riddle with a red bean riddle, one can change negation into affirmation. By using these kinds of methods to guess the mystery of the current situation, one can probably tear off this piece of riddle paper.

For example, the diplomat's set phrase "Absolutely no humiliation," is a mystery of the current situation. The first step is to use the reversed riddle and the bell-tied riddle to guess it, that is, "humiliation does not decide;" so it is clear that the diplomat cannot resolve the words humiliation. The second step is to use the bell-tied riddle with a red bean riddle to guess it, the word "no" tied with a bell, becomes the word "negation:" and using the red bean riddle to divide one sentence into two sentences, the form is like: "Is there humiliation? Deciding." "Is there humiliation?" is a question; the word "deciding" is an answer, it means deciding to be humiliated; then negation becomes affirmation.

Let's guess two more mysteries of the current situation: for example, the soldiers' "Absolutely no retreat," using a reversed riddle, becomes "Letting retreat does not decide." Using a bell-tied riddle with a red bean riddle, it becomes "Letting retreat? Deciding." Another example, the important people's "Absolutely no peace talks," using a reversed riddle, becomes "Peace talks not decided." Using a bell-tied riddle with a red bean riddle, it becomes "Peace talks? Deciding."

How sad this is! Is there humiliation? Deciding. Is there retreat? Deciding. Are there peace talks? Deciding. Alas! Such is the mystery of the current situation.

Rural Bankruptcy

— Yongzi

The countryside is bankrupt, the farmers all throw down their hoes and iron shovels and sneak into the city. If the people in the city, besides the foreign relief wheat, will soon have no food to eat, what will they do?

Rural bankruptcy is really not a fashionable thing. I remember when I still had a small pigtail tied with red velvet rope, there was already a large group, a large group of famine refugees, coming from north of the river, thousands of miles away, to the south of the river. Is this not ironclad proof that rural bankruptcy was already all the rage twenty or thirty years ago? These famine refugees have continued to come to my hometown every year until now. Nothing has changed much from twenty years ago, and we still eat three meals of white rice every day. So rural bankruptcy, even if it goes bankrupt, there's no need to panic.

But we eat three meals of white rice every day, and if we have some leisure time, then we might as well study the problem of rural bankruptcy, if necessary.

I remember when I used to visit the famine refugees in the countryside, there were often several old men with the faces of lords, wearing tan leather robes and velvet vests, sitting in sedan chairs, in each group, and I was very puzzled. Later, I found out that these were all wealthy households, what are now called big landlords. Wealthy households had inexhaustible rice and inexhaustible money. No matter how bankrupt the tenant farmers were, they could not break the wealthy households, but the tenant farmers said that if the wealthy households did not flee the famine, everyone would eat the wealthy households, and the wealthy households could not bear to pull a hair to benefit the tenant farmers, so they had to sit in sedan chairs and flee the famine.

Since then, everyone has been shouting the slogan of saving the villages, but I don't know how the honorable committee members will start. The peasants have no organization, and to provide relief, it is inevitable that they will have to connect with the sedan chair-sitting famine refugees who have the qualifications of gentry directors. Oh, that's how it's done. Those who sit in two-person sedan chairs are afraid that they will greatly get some grease, and change to sitting in four-person sedan chairs. Rural bankruptcy, that's really bankrupt.

By then, we will probably have to replace our three meals of white rice with relief wheat.

Funeral

— Chonglou

In the city, I often see magnificent funerals.

In front are swaggering cavalry, bands in red and green uniforms, walking teams carrying various sacrificial offerings, monk and Taoist teams with yellow faces and dark nights due to opium smoking, followed by bands and walking teams..., and all people and objects, winding and advancing!

The filial sons (?) are walking in front of the coffin, although they say they are "stupefied and delirious, in unbearable pain." But they have not forgotten to send a few bodyguards to protect them in case of accidents due to walking.

The funeral cars followed slowly behind the procession, as if they had lost their authority to speed. However, in this kind of disharmonious situation, you can hear the crowded onlookers laughing and cheering beside you and saying, "This is a very good-looking grand funeral!"

The person is already dead, but the person's bones are still being used as a tool for a funeral! Someone said, "The dead are often deceived by the living," and I believe it even more after watching the funeral.

A Record of the Mirage in Qingdao

— Zhuying

In the sea off Qingdao, in the undulating mountains and rocks fifty li from the shore, in a place called Maizuru Beach, at half past eleven at noon on May 22, a strange sight suddenly appeared: pavilions and towers, higher than the mountain peaks, the so-called mirage. The buildings looked like two large-scale factories, with windows and doors open and people walking back and forth. In this instant, even the work of gods could not be so fast, but now it suddenly appeared before our eyes.

At that time, my friend Mr. Qu Yisan was strolling on the fine sand of the beach. When he saw this strange sight, he was shocked and thought he had never seen it in his life. He wanted to call me by phone to share this spectacle that had not been seen for thousands of years, but there was no phone there. So he sent Mr. Mou, who was traveling with him, to send a letter to my residence. I was napping when I suddenly heard the news. I hurriedly went, and when I arrived, I saw that the mirage in the sea had gradually dissipated, only about ten feet from the water line.

The buildings were light ochre in color, no different from the mountains and rocks, lying flat on the water. Sails came and went on the water, making it difficult to distinguish between real and illusion. At that time, some tourists on the beach hired fishing boats to go and see the strange sight, but they sank when they reached the spot and returned in disappointment. Behind the buildings was a city wall, and in front were trees, like the scene of Qianmen in Beijing. On the left was a small pavilion, with white clouds gushing high below it, like an ancient painting hanging deep in the sea and sky, no wonder the viewers praised it as a miracle.

Since the news of the appearance of the mirage spread, people on Zhongshan Road rushed to see it, and the road was blocked. Everyone scrambled to be first, some by rickshaw, some by motorcycle, and some by bicycle. Cars and horses came and went, rushing and bumping, regardless of everything, for fear of missing it.

As a result, a group of superstitious people started rumors, some saying what would happen to Qingdao, some saying what would happen to the overall situation. The general residents were surprised and their opinions were divided. Others said that it was a mirage opening its abdomen and exposing its scales, using the sunlight to dry them, and reflecting the scenery of the buildings on the shore into the scales, and from the scales, reflecting them onto the shore. Others said that if they could take out the pearls and gems from its belly and set them as lamps and candles, and burn them with fire at night, they would see the buildings floating in the candlelight, as if they were appearing in the sea. Although the words were unfounded, they were enough to comfort the longing of those who had not seen it.

The beach was crowded with people, with thousands of heads moving. The rocks on both sides of Nanhai Shimen were blocked by viewers, with no room to insert a foot. Everyone scrambled to see this rare sight of a century, but the good times did not last long, and in a blink of an eye (after about an hour) it was no longer visible. As a result, those who came later could only sigh in disappointment. Unable to see this spectacle, they all hoped that it would reappear on the sea at this time tomorrow, so they could enjoy it to the fullest, but it could not be as people wished.

According to the theory, a mirage is entirely the result of atmospheric effects. The temperature is lower than the air, and after several refractions, it reflects the scenery of palaces and cities, appearing faintly and reflecting into people's eyes. This phenomenon often occurs in the spring and summer, when the wind is calm and the waves are gentle.

Letter to the Editor I read Mr. Zheng Jun Yimei's anecdote about Lu Zijia in your newspaper yesterday, and it is quite different from the truth. It must be a mistake in the transmission. I have been in Lu's staff for a long time. It is not necessary to pursue the rights and wrongs of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang war, but Lu never advocated war. He twice secretly instructed me to come to Shanghai and ask Mr. Tang Shaochuan to find a way to mediate from the side. Mr. Shaochuan is still alive and can be questioned. As for whether there was any appropriation of military pay from Xia Chao or slapping, it has not been ten years, and the gentry in Zhejiang should be able to recall it, so I don't need to defend it on his behalf. According to the investigation, Lu's father disappeared during the Boxer Rebellion in the Gengzi year. Although most of what a certain tabloid reported yesterday was inconsistent, the disappearance was indeed a fact. His mother had already passed away before the Jiangsu-Zhejiang war, so how could there be a mother? As for Lu's never having jewels and antiques, and never speaking harshly to his subordinates, anyone who has even one day of acquaintance with Lu can say this. As for what this attendant said, I don't know what he saw that made him say that. I hope you will examine and reveal the truth. Respectfully, Liao An

Miscellaneous Talk

News on the Lake

— Tianxu Wosheng

Since the invasion of rayon, the Chinese silk industry has declined rapidly, because the prices are so different, the buyers are greedy for cheap goods, and the merchants value profits. These eight words have become an incurable disease. After the January 28th Incident last year, I had several articles in the Machine Alliance, expressing my views, hoping that the price of natural silk could compete with rayon. Unexpectedly, the real silk brocade sold at the Hangzhou National Goods Exhibition this time was actually cheaper than rayon. Each piece was only fourteen yuan, four yards and six feet long and two feet four inches wide, only about three corners per foot. The lowest price for rayon brocade was three corners and four cents per foot. Therefore, I cut one strip of each and burned them with a match. The real silk only felt scorched and swollen, like opium paste, and did not turn into ash. The rayon, on the other hand, was no different from cloth strips, and immediately turned into flying ash. If rayon and natural silk are interwoven and burned, the truth and falsehood are also obvious and cannot be hidden. Therefore, I think this kind of testing method is very simple, everyone can try it on the spot, and everyone can identify it. Our Hangzhou has this beautiful and cheap product, how can other places not? If it can be like this, not only can rayon be defeated, but also foreign yarn can be defeated, because cloth woven with fine yarn is called domestic, but it is actually spun from foreign cotton. Among the 500 million yuan of excess imports, cotton, rice and wheat are only three items. If everyone rejects fine cloth and uses big brocade, there is no danger of excess spiritual silk and there is no need to sell it abroad. This kind of big brocade, in terms of its labor and capital, even if it is sold for three corners a foot, is only a strategy of small profits and quick turnover, and it will not lead to losses. The average weight of each bolt is only one pound and seventy-five. Calculated at a silk price of 640 yuan per dan, the raw materials used are only eight yuan and four corners. The weaving cost is one corner per foot, only four yuan and six corners. Even the profits earned by the sellers have exceeded the normal rate of five percent and cannot be said to be too thin. On the user side, it can be said to be the most affordable. The price of foreign cloth still needs more than two corners per foot, so why not use this big brocade instead of buying foreign cloth? If cloth must be used, then domestic cloth should be purchased to avoid the outflow of rights and interests. But if everyone holds this purpose, then the two items of rayon and American cotton can be resolved, and the revival of the countryside can be awaited. Really looking forward to it.

Club

— Zhou Cailiang

Speaking of clubs, everyone knows they are places for leisure and entertainment. Examining the origin of this term, it is indeed an authentic product from the East. Initially, only the major commercial ports in our country had them, and the members were mostly Chinese who served foreign merchants. Whenever there were holidays, the members would arrive as agreed. All kinds of elegant entertainment facilities, such as string and bamboo music, books and newspapers, and chess (tea is a given), were almost all available. The so-called "catering to individual preferences" allowed everyone to relax and enjoy themselves, which was truly beneficial in alleviating work fatigue and refreshing the spirit. Later, as the trend opened up and more people imitated, the quality of the members became uneven. As a result, gambling entertainment like "mahjong" gradually became popular. As time passed, it slowly encroached upon the club's primary function. Moreover, because the club's organization was a legitimate group, it seemed that the authorities tacitly allowed it to enjoy the special privilege of guaranteeing gambling safety. Where there is profit, everyone will be envious and imitate. Not to mention distant places, let's just take my hometown (Zhangxi), a remote coastal area, as an example. In a small town with less than a thousand households, there are forty or fifty teahouses and taverns that provide entertainment (not including tobacco). Among them, the disguised gambling dens of clubs are the most prevalent. Even during the busy farming season, people are still gambling day and night. From the gentry class to the laborers, whether they know each other or not, they almost all revel in it. Ordinarily, this would mean that the market would be somewhat prosperous, and the farmers' lives would be unusually comfortable. But the reality is quite the opposite. It is said that since the salt harvest last autumn, due to the cheap grain hurting farmers, the pawnshop business, which regulates the economy of the common people, has plummeted (more pawns than redemptions). The sluggishness of other businesses is also imaginable. So, the fact that the business of clubs (taking my hometown as an example) is exclusively prosperous is actually accelerating the collapse of the entire rural economy. Alas! I never thought that after decades of revolution and education in our country, the result has been the popularization of mahjong education everywhere. Since the people are so fond of pleasure, how can the national affairs not fall into a state of "Isn't it delightful?" Alas! What can I say!

Full Length Novel

The Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Eight: Indignant Words Stir Youth to Resign and Flee;

Passionate Compassion for a Maiden Leads to a Grave Visit.

Zhao Ziqiang, in the heat of wine and excitement, suddenly changed the subject and mentioned the old Mrs. Yang in the front yard. Guan Yaowu felt that his suggestion couldn't be without meaning, so he immediately went to the front yard to meet Mrs. Jiang. In the courtyard, he first shouted, "Happy New Year!" and then pushed the door open and went into the house. Mrs. Jiang greeted him with a smile, "Cousin is here. Guizhi, quickly make tea." Guizhi responded and came out. Today, she was wearing a brand-new patterned cheongsam. Following the customs of the Manchu people, she still had a long braid. In front of her forehead, she had long bangs, which showed that even though she was over twenty years old, she still retained her virgin beauty. Although her face was painted with thick powder like other Manchu girls, her skin was much more delicate than ordinary people. When she smiled, her red lips revealed two rows of white teeth, which were beauties that other girls over twenty could not have. Guan Yaowu immediately thought, "With such a good girl, and able to do both rough and fine work, what else could my brother not want? It's just that because of the neighborly relationship, it's hard to bring it up." Then again, a talent like Cousin should at least marry someone like Zhao Ziqiang to be worthy of her. In the instant Guan Yaowu entered the door, looking at Guizhi's face, he had already turned over several thoughts. Guizhi, seeing him paying so much attention, felt a little embarrassed and couldn't help but lower her head. She picked up the teapot, poured tea, and said, "What's wrong? Cousin is staring at me today. Is there anything special about my face today?" Guan Yaowu smiled, "I can read faces. I see that the stars of romance and marriage are shining on your face. Good news is coming." Guizhi placed a cup of tea on the old tea table and pushed it in front of him. With a pout, she said, "It's the first month of the year, say something good." Guan Yaowu tilted his head and looked at her, saying, "Is 'stars of romance and marriage are shining on your face' bad? Do you know what the stars of romance and marriage are?" (85)

The title of Chapter 7, "Drinking Wine and Talking 'High'" has "High" mistakenly printed as "Merchant"

Free Talk

Further Discussion on "Force-feeding" Education

— Tianyi

The other day, someone talked about education from the perspective of force-feeding, saying that educators today are mostly doing the work of force-feeding. Teachers are unwilling to consider students' interests, nor do they consider the needs of the current society and era. They only squeeze a bunch of so-called "knowledge" as food and cram it into students' bellies. Once the students' bellies are full, they consider their only responsibility fulfilled. This analogy is certainly very harsh, but I think that if the teachers today really had a bunch of "knowledge" as food in their hands, and could really fill the students' bellies like force-feeding a duck, then it would still be considered passable. But the fact is that most teachers today never had food in their hands in the first place. The reason why they "tirelessly teach" is not to fill the students' bellies, but only to fill their own bellies.

If we do not deny the facts, we must admit that the educators of today, the superiors are acting as magicians, the middling ones are like playing gramophones, and the inferior ones are simply using students as tools for food and clothing. What is meant by acting as magicians? Today, they move in Eastern systems, and tomorrow, they boast about European and American doctrines. They change old-fashioned essays without seeking to adapt to reality, and without seeking any efficiency. Just like performing magic tricks, the performers only show off their novelty and boast about their cleverness. What is meant by playing gramophones? The sound emitted by a gramophone is only a passive action, a mechanical call, simply chanting stereotyped songs. Many teachers are also like this, teaching only for the sake of teaching, without any purpose. Education cannot be used in a lively way, and becomes a dead and clumsy "form," or a tool for decorating the eyes and ears. As for using students as tools for food and clothing, the fact is even more obvious, and we don't need to elaborate here. Because education is like this, the result of education is only to cultivate high-level idlers for society, and to create bureaucrats and politicians for the country. Although force-feeding education does not have positive benefits for society, the negative harm is also relatively small. However, this kind of force-feeding education is also rare today!

Don't Cry!

— Ma Guoliang

Perhaps some people have never enjoyed a moment of happiness from birth to death, but no one has never experienced pain, whether directly from the spirit or indirectly from material things.

There are many kinds of pain, and we seem unable to use objective and fixed standards to measure and say which kind of pain is deeper or shallower. This varies from person to person, from time to time, and from place to place. Just like a child losing his favorite toy, and a rich man losing his wealth, who can say which of these two people is suffering more?

But although we cannot say which type of pain is the lightest, we can say which type of pain is the greatest. This is the pain of "having pain but not being allowed to express it."

A child loses his toy and is not allowed to cry, a rich man loses his wealth and is not allowed to sigh, or complain to others. Is there any pain in the world that is deeper than this?

In everyday life, when we encounter misfortune, we will definitely find a friend, or a relative who can sympathize with us, to tell them the troubles that are suppressed in our hearts. Although this does not help the facts, it makes us feel much better when we have the opportunity to pour it out. This is an experience that everyone has had. If you can't find someone to talk to, just cry out loud, or vent through writing, books, or music. These are all methods people usually use to vent their pain. Chuan Baicun's so-called art is a symbol of suffering, is what this means.

As for the father being killed, the son goes through all kinds of hardships to kill the enemy. In fact, it is clear that killing the enemy cannot bring the dead father back to life. There is no other reason than to vent the pain caused by the father's murder. To take a more ordinary example, someone breaks a vase in their home because they are extremely angry. We cannot laugh at them for being stupid. Only the smartest people can think of breaking a vase to relieve the pain when they are in so much pain that they cannot vent it.

From this, it can be seen that although people have no way to resist the coming of pain, they know how to get rid of it after it comes. If even the right to get rid of pain is deprived, isn't that the most unbearable thing? Mansfield, in her "Ma Parker," said that this old woman has tasted all the tragedies of life, but doesn't even have a place where she can cry to her heart's content. Life to this point is truly more tragic than death!

Recently, I read Oliver Goldsmith's "Happiness In a Great Measure Dependen On Constitution," which, when talking about how to resist pain, he said, "... the first method is to forget our troubles, and the next method is to hide our troubles; fighting with misfortune, we will definitely be injured in the conflict. The only way to achieve victory is to escape."

What he calls "escape" is to forget or hide the pain. In fact, whether or not one can forget is not up to them, and hiding is just deceiving oneself. The pain is still accumulated in the heart, and one is still suffering and seeking a way to vent and get rid of it.

This morning, looking out the window, I saw my neighbor whipping a young maid. Just as the little girl cried loudly in pain, the stern mistress said, "Don't cry!" I thought for the child that she was unable to forget the humiliation and physical pain she had suffered. And "hiding" it was of no use to her at all. Indeed, she cried again in the end! But what followed the cry was another roar of "Don't cry!" and whipping!

This miserable world!

Regret

— Lin Huiyin

Like sharks cannot live without the sea, I, who grew up in a tea-drinking land, am always looking for places to drink tea. In Nanjing, Yuhuatai is one of the places I often go to drink tea.

One time, after sitting and drinking enough, I walked out of the teahouse and went up along the winding path. At the top, I saw a place where there was no one, as if it was a forgotten solitary grave, standing there alone and desolate. My direction of advance was focused on that side. Just as I was going up that slope, I suddenly heard shouts from behind. The sound disturbed my focused steps. I couldn't hear what they were shouting. But because they were shouting so fiercely, I couldn't help but stop and turn around to investigate. When I turned back, I saw a soldier standing on the opposite hill, holding his gun flat in both hands, in the pose of about to pull the trigger. It seemed that my body or part of it was the target of his soon-to-be-fired bullet.

"If you go any further, I'll shoot you!" the soldier roared.

At this time, I was surprised to see that the soldier's shouting was indeed directed at me. I looked puzzledly at the small house at the end of the hill I wanted to go to.

"Still looking! Do you want to be cannon fodder?" the soldier warned and questioned, as if he didn't understand either.

"Oh, so there is a cannon there. If I go, I will be 'cannon fodder'." I woke up and thoughtfully descended the slope I had climbed. I also paid attention to see if I had overlooked signs like "Fortress Area, No Entry" on the side of the road. But there were none. "What if I hadn't turned back just now!" I thought again; "If I hadn't turned back just now, no, perhaps I would have reached the other shore of life. A realm completely different from my current one?"

No; I didn't want to commit suicide. It's just that taking life so unknowingly, or even suffering some small injuries, always feels like a more meaningful thing, although if that were really the case, someone might calmly say that it was a stupid thing to walk to such a dangerous place as a fortress without thinking.

Yes, I regret my nosy head for once.

Ramblings from a Humble Cottage

— Zizhan

(Thirty-Seven) Time to Rest

Yesterday (May 27th), a small Shanghai newspaper published a short article titled "It is Said," written by a woman claiming to be Ms. Yunying. It roughly said, "Freedom Talk once declared that it would accept public submissions... Even Mr. Zizhan's, the stinky and rotten gentleman of the eighteenth century, posthumous work, Ramblings from a Humble Cottage, is published above. Alas, Zizhan, such works, time to rest." After I finished reading it, I couldn't help but exclaim, "Ms. Yunying! Such works, I am not yet willing to rest. My writing has no great meaning, it's just for eating. To hold me accountable for a famous mountain cause, how dare I? To call it stinky and rotten, I am still too humble to accept. Someone scolded me for being incompetent, I respectfully thanked them and said, I am indeed incompetent, what is there to be lower than? Someone scolded me for not being revolutionary, I also respectfully thanked them and said, why revolution? I have no comrades. Someone ridiculed me for being outdated, I laughed and replied, I have already landed. Someone ridiculed me for being old-fashioned, I also laughed and said, I am already old-fashioned for the winter. Yet another person criticized me for having a musty brain, I said, for a person to be musty, it's not just the brain. Now Ms. Yunying says that I am an eighteenth-century person, but in fact, I seek to be a person of the age of Wu Huai, a person of the age of Ge Tian, but I cannot obtain it. A talks about the materialistic view of history, saying it is a panacea; B talks about the people's livelihood view of history, saying it can eliminate all diseases; I talk about the eating view of history, it's just everyday food. My teaching is not for the high name of a university professor, it's just for cheating food. My writing is not to call myself an author, it's just for cheating food. I certainly do not wish to know what era I was born in, Qin? Han? Or modern times? Let others decide."

Carrot Hair

— Written by Jules Renaro, Translated by Lin Qu

Like Brutus (continued)

Mrs. Lepic: How is that? You made such a loud speech, your face flushed, waving your fists, almost shouting so that the whole village could hear, and you still say you didn't say anything! Say that sentence again and let everyone listen.

Carrot Hair: There's no need to say it again. Let it go, Mom.

Mrs. Lepic: Say it, say it, who were you talking about just now; who exactly were you talking about?

Carrot Hair: You wouldn't understand this person, Mom.

Mrs. Lepic: That's exactly why I want you to say it. I ask you to clear your head a little bit, and then obey my words.

Carrot Hair: Okay, I'll say it! Mom, just now I was chatting with Dad, and Dad gave me some kind advice. Because I wanted to express my gratitude to Dad, I don't know where the idea came from, but I actually made a promise in front of Dad, and quoted the words of that Roman called Brutus...

Mrs. Lepic: Bah, you're talking nonsense. I ask you to repeat that sentence you said just now in the same tone, word for word. I feel that what I'm asking for isn't anything extraordinary, and you really can consider your mother's feelings and do it.

Felix: Can I repeat it for him, Mom?

Mrs. Lepic: No, let him say it first, then you say it, and then we'll compare. Say it, Carrot Hair, hurry up.

Carrot Hair said in a voice that was about to cry, stuttering.

"Oh… integrity… you… are… just… a… noun…"

Mrs. Lepic: There's really no way. This thing can't be said no matter what. He would rather be beaten than make his mother happy.

Felix: Listen, Mom, he said it like this… (He turned his eyes around, casting a provocative look.) "If I don't get first place on my essay," (He puffed out his cheeks and stomped his feet on the ground.) "I can write like Brutus…" (He raised his arms.) "Oh, integrity!" (He put down his arms.) "You are just a noun!" That's what he said.

Mrs. Lepic: Very good, learned it perfectly! I congratulate you, Carrot Hair, but you insisted on not repeating it, which is really a pity for me, because imitation is ultimately not as good as the original.

Felix: But, Carrot Hair, did Brutus actually say this? Isn't this what Cato said?

Carrot Hair: I believe it was definitely Brutus who said it. The book also said... "Afterwards, he threw himself on the sword in his friend's hand and committed suicide."

Elesdin: Carrot Hair is right. I still remember that Brutus pretended to be crazy and stuffed gold into his cane.

Carrot Hair: No, Sister, you're mixed up. You've mixed up the Brutus I'm talking about with another person.

Elesdin: But I believe it won't be wrong. I can guarantee you that what Ms. Sophie taught us about history will never be worse than what your public middle school teacher taught.

Mrs. Lepic: That's irrelevant. Don't argue. The most important thing is that we have to have a Brutus in our family, and we already have one now. Thanks to Carrot Hair's efforts, we can make people envy us! We don't even know how glorious it is to have this. Now you can look at this new Brutus. He speaks Latin like a bishop, but he refuses to give a second mass to the deaf. Turn him over and look at him from the front, the new clothes he put on today already have stains, and look at him from the back, his pants are already torn. Heavens, where did he run off to again? No, let me beat the Carrot Hair who has become Brutus and show you! Young beast, get lost!

Finance

Interbank Rate Varies Between Morning and Afternoon

Yesterday, the foreign interbank rate suddenly varied between the morning and afternoon sessions, with the morning rate at five points and the afternoon rate at three points. This was the first time since the foreign interbank rate was adopted that the morning and afternoon rates differed on the same day, as usually the rate is the same for both sessions. Regarding banks, the banks on the Bund had a holiday closure on the day before yesterday due to the Dragon Boat Festival, which coincided with a Sunday, so they had to make up for the holiday closure yesterday. However, the Central Bank and the Customs Office were open as usual, and the Chinese banks did not make up for the holiday either. It is estimated that they received more than 600,000 yuan in ticket payments and about 2 million yuan in various freight, tax, and miscellaneous payments. Due to the holiday closure the day before yesterday, the amount of money collected by the money shops for foreign public orders increased, with a total of more than 43 million yuan, more than 400,000 yuan in remittances from various routes, and 200,000 yuan in remittances from customers. In the interbank ticket trading, the morning session had more than 4.7 million yuan in transfers and 780,000 yuan in new transactions, the afternoon session had more than 400,000 yuan in transactions, and the small general association had more than 500,000 yuan in transactions. Banknote inflows and outflows amounted to more than 1.1 million yuan. In addition, the total amount exchanged at the clearing house on the 29th was 2,513,846.93 yuan in silver dollars. Among them, the Bund banks were closed for a holiday, so there was no exchange of silver dollars. The total amount of silver dollars remitted was 2,513,846.93 yuan.

Both Jiangsu and Guangdong Coins Rise

Yesterday, the Jiangsu small silver coin was 854.5 yuan in the morning session and 853 yuan in the afternoon session. Although there was a small difference of 1.5 yuan between the two sessions, it seemed to have risen by more than 2 yuan compared to the price at the end of last week. The trading volume was 5,000 coins in the morning session and 7,000 coins in the afternoon session. The Guangdong small silver coin was 778.5 yuan in the morning session and 777.5 yuan in the afternoon session. As a result, it was also 2.5 yuan higher than the previous day. The trading volume was 75,000 coins in the morning session and 45,000 coins in the afternoon session. Copper coins remained unchanged at 317,500 coins. The trading volume was 38,100 strings, with a total value of 12,000 yuan in foreign currency.

The Beiyang Coins Will be Used Directly From Now On

In the past, the most commonly used silver coins were the Yuan head and Sun Yat-sen coins. Among other old coins, such as the British coin, Jiangsu coin, and Guangdong dragon coin, there was liquidity, but the Beiyang coin was not very applicable in the market. Money shops often had to charge a discount, which was very inconvenient. After the unification of silver coins this time, measures should be taken to curb the miscellaneous foreign coins that require a discount. Therefore, the Chinese and foreign banking associations recently held a joint meeting and, with the consent of the leaders of the money industry, decided to use the Beiyang coin directly. All money shops and banks should use this coin directly when opening boxes and encountering it in their inventory, without the need for exchange, to facilitate convenience. It was announced yesterday that a notice has been posted in the financial market to inform the entire society.

Large, Long-Term Loans at 625

National News Agency, London, 29th. Large, long-term loans at 625. The recent price is 18 pence 9375, and the forward price is 19 pence. The British-American exchange rate opened at 3 yuan 9 jiao 7 fen 25.

Securities

Peaceful Progress

Government Bonds Showed Weak Upward Momentum Last Week

| Increase from several jiao to two yuan |

From May 22nd to 27th last week, the bond market of the Chinese Securities Exchange was very tense. The mystery of Tianjin and Beijing was confusing, and after several weeks, it was finally broken on Wednesday last week. The short sellers were almost on the verge of desperation at this point, but their reaction did not affect the stop-loss limit, because the short sellers had prepared to some extent. Therefore, the escape of Tianjin and Beijing from the crisis was fortunate, and there was no violent storm. Only with the arrival of peaceful news, after the newspapers were published, the trend suddenly became strange and unpredictable, and the speculators were able to do their best. When the news spread throughout the market, it became calm and quiet. How the situation will change in the future depends on the negotiations. On Monday last week, the situation in Tianjin and Beijing was already felt to be imminent, and the situation in North China was extremely chaotic. Large investors even sold out, and the market price fell from 34 jiao to 1 yuan 1 jiao 5 fen. On Tuesday, according to newspaper reports, the atmosphere of peace seemed to be a bubble. The morning session even fell by 67 jiao, with a downward trend. Unexpectedly, at the close of the market, news of a ceasefire suddenly filled the market. For a time, the bulls were jubilant, and the short sellers were extremely panicked. The Northern Gang first rushed to cover their positions, and all gangs bravely bought in. In one session, the market price soared by 23 yuan. The trading volume was also very brisk, and the closing time in the afternoon was already 5 o'clock. The closing sale reached 9 o'clock. Because this day was the last day of the first half of May, the number of outstanding positions could not be reduced, and the trading volume reached more than 27.4 million, creating the highest trading volume record this year. On Wednesday, only the June session was being collected, and because the accounts on Tuesday were extremely confusing, there was one session in the morning and afternoon, and the market price rose slightly by half a yuan or so. On Thursday, the July futures session began to be traded, but the trading volume was greatly reduced, and the market price was slightly sluggish by about 4 jiao. On Friday, the delivery of the May futures was carried out, and trading was suspended for one day. On Saturday, because the preliminary peace had been completed, except for one or two large investors who still sold, the demand from others was still urgent, and the market price continued to rise by 34 jiao to 1 yuan 1 jiao. In summary, the market price rose from several jiao to 2 yuan for the whole week. The total trading volume was 72,948,000 yuan, including 38,000 yuan in spot goods. The futures stamp duty alone amounted to 17,175,000 yuan, the demobilization accounted for 12,450,000 yuan, the unified tax accounted for 10,150,000 yuan, the 19 customs duty accounted for 11,490,000 yuan, the 20-volume 20-customs duty accounted for 16,115,000 yuan, and the rest ranged from several hundred thousand to 230,000 yuan.

New Tea Weighing in Wuyuan is Not Brisk

Since Wuyuan green tea opened at a new price of 40 to 45 yuan on the 19th, various companies have been negotiating prices based on the market. Considering the poor market conditions for both black and green tea, tea companies were timid and hesitant to proceed. They still hoped to lower the mountain price of 40 yuan. There are still not many others who have opened for weighing without prices. Companies that suffered heavy losses last year and those that are financially sound are mostly watching and not proceeding. Tea assistants have been sent out to collect scales and return to the villages. The coldness of the market is truly rare.

Xiushui Black Tea Production Suffers Losses

In Xun, the price offered for Xiushui's early black tea ranges from 700 to 1,000 cash per catty, equivalent to 30 yuan in foreign currency per dan, a decrease of more than 20 yuan compared to last year. The cost of the first batch of boxed tea is around 100 yuan. The mountain price has opened at only 20 to 10 yuan. Because the number of tea companies in the mountains has decreased this year, there is no competition to inflate prices, so mountain prices have been immediately lowered. The production of Xiutong tea this year has suffered significant losses, reaching only 40-50% of last year's production. The second batch of boxed tea from various companies is already being shipped. Because the tea from the third batch is coarse and old, few companies are processing it. Companies with small amounts of tea can complete their operations within the month. In total, the output of boxed tea from Xiudi this year will not exceed 3,000 to 4,000 boxes. The shortfall in tea output is significantly different from the past. (May 23)

Qimen Tea Reaches a New Low Price

Yesterday, the road for Qimen, Fuliang, and Jiande black tea and Yingde Zhuang was slightly active. However, the British telegrams set extremely strict price limits. The cost of the first batch of goods was relatively high, and negotiations between Chinese and foreign parties were difficult to approach. The goods traded were mostly the second batch of tea recently arrived, totaling 2,124 boxes of black tea and 445 boxes of green tea. The market price for Qimen tea has already opened to the lowest price of 80 yuan, and the situation remains unfavorable. After a drop last week, Zun'an Tuzhuang Zhenmei green tea was not opened. The Tunxi New Tribute was also lowered by the Baitouzhuang Yu Jiang foreign firm, with a price of 100 yuan, only 85% lower than last year. The overall trend of the tea market is said to be better for green tea than black tea.

Ningzhou Tea Market Depressed

The Ning black tea of the past was once famous, dominating the tea market. Recently, it has almost disappeared and is barely surviving. The tea market here is showing a depressed atmosphere again this year. The following is based on the findings of the investigation: The tea companies in Xiushui and Wuning counties in Tiaoshui County include Jichang, Guangxinglong, Zhonghechang, Zhentailong, Hengfengshun, Yuanfengxiang, Shengfa, Yuanfeng Yiji, Yuji, Shengji, Jinfengchang, Yutaiheng, Hengfenglong, Zhengdayuan (the above sell to Shanghai Zhuangkou), Chunji, Tongyu, Hengchun, Gonghelong, and Wusongji (the above sell to Nanchang Zhuangkou), a total of 20 companies. Except for Jichang and Guangxinglong, which also make green tea boxes and baskets, the rest specialize in making black tea baskets. Those in Wuning County include Shendasheng, Huangwanshun, Tangzhengxing, Fangmingchun, Yitaifu, Yuxingxiang, Gongshengchang, and Qingchanglong, a total of eight companies that specialize in making black tea baskets and sell them to Shanghai. There are also more than ten other companies, including Shiyuxing, Dajixiang, Qianheyu, Chunsheng, Yihefu, Qianyulong, Rongtaixiang, Yufulong, Ruifenglong, Deji, Yuanhexing, and Shichanglong, distributed in various towns of Xiuwu. In total, the tea that has been imported by various companies in Xiushui this year includes 832 pieces in baskets, 6,085 pieces in bags, and 14 pieces in boxes. As for Wuning, the exact number has not yet been found, so it is not listed.

Current Situation of Xiushui Tea Industry Improvement Farm

The Tea Industry Improvement Farm jointly organized by the Central Agricultural Experiment of the Ministry of Industry and the Shanghai and Wuhan Commodity Inspection Bureaus is located at the old site of the Ning Tea Revitalization Company in Baipengkeng, Xiushui. The company was originally founded by Chen, a giant merchant in the tea industry, with a large scale and owning more than 2,000 mu of vast tea mountains. However, due to poor management, it suffered losses every year, amounting to hundreds of thousands. Recently, due to local unrest, there was no intention to continue, so the Ministry of Industry leased and took over the establishment of the Tea Industry Improvement Farm, and appointed Yu Haiqing as the person in charge. After receiving the order, Yu arrived at the farm with technical staff in late last month to handle the handover and preparation matters. As it was the tea season, on the one hand, they worked day and night to manufacture. Currently, the first batch of products from the farm has been manufactured into dozens of boxes, with very good quality. The shape, color, and aroma far exceed Qihong. It is said that if it were not affected by time and machinery, the results would be more than this. The batch of tea leaves will be shipped to Shanghai soon, and the second batch is currently being rushed, which can also be packed and shipped out within about a week.

Commentary

Blood

— Ox

Blood is truly an ominous thing. Bloodshed in Shanghai can be said to happen every day, and today's special bloodbath commemoration on Nanjing Road is enough to show that blood is an ominous sign. Extending this by hundreds of steps, the bloodletting of January 28th, the bloodbath of September 18th, and even the recent bloodshed in Peiping and Tianjin, the bloodshed between Liu and Deng in Sichuan, our country's ardent sons, I don't know how many heads have been thrown, how much hot blood has been thickened. When you talk about blood, you really can't help but feel cold.

Blood is originally an ominous thing. Historically, when a country has many events and is about to stir up war, there are often reports of "blood rain" and "red rivers." Heaven first warns of it. Especially in recent years, changes have occurred repeatedly. For example, near Longmen last year, the Yellow River suddenly narrowed, and treasures, rice, and grain were turned up in the river. These kinds of changes are naturally not good omens. According to a Shantou telegram, a rainbow circled the sun in Chao'an for half an hour, and the water in the Chao River turned red, and the sand and mud boiled up, turbid like blood. From Zhuzhen Mountain to Jishuitacheng, people changed to drinking well water. It took twenty hours to put it out. Isn't this a kind of blood report? The blood cases in the north are not dry, and the blood signs in the south have appeared again. It's true that the bloodshed won't stop.

However, people in Shanghai's lower society often regard money as blood. For example, they say, "I originally wanted to treat guests today, but there is no blood in the purse," or "So-and-so's blood is Mecca Mecca, but unfortunately, they are unwilling to pluck a hair." They often use blood to replace money. At first, I didn't understand. Money is auspicious and precious, while blood is the most terrible and miserable thing. It seems inappropriate to compare money to blood.

Thinking carefully, there is a great truth in it. The human body's blood is originally the most precious. If a person has no blood, then their heart is dead. Money is also the most precious thing to people. If people have no money, they cannot live. Therefore, what is miserable and terrible is blood, and what is most precious is also blood. What is lovely and precious is money, and what is terrible and miserable is also money. Therefore, comparing blood to money is truly an apt and clever metaphor.

Heroes on the road draw sharp knives for a few yuan, causing bloodshed. Imperialists take airplanes and cannons and run rampant everywhere, also causing bloodshed. Therefore, money is the price of blood, and blood is also the price of money. If money is used improperly, it is indeed a waste. If it is not used when it should be used, it is also "dying wronged."

It is the same with blood. If it is not shed when it should not be shed, it will not flourish. If it is not shed when it should be shed, how can it be "living in humiliation"?

If blood capital is sacrificed and money is won, there is no loss for both sides. If blood capital is sacrificed and no money is won, it is a true sacrifice of blood capital for a big sale. And on the customer side, the goods are obtained, but no money is paid. Where can such a bargain be found? Therefore, bleeding without getting a price is a true "death of injustice," and getting a price without bleeding is only "robbery."

It's Hard for "God"!

— Ai Lian

In a city where people are in a panic, news comes that the soldiers are approaching the city. The tragic and painful past images are trembling in everyone's hearts. If the facts are about to be revealed, what else can comfort the heart? "Um! Pray, or pray to God for help!" So the whole family ran to the statue of the Virgin, and the elder began to pray... "Heavenly Father! We thank you for the food, clothing, and shelter you have given us; our souls can be resurrected, and our sins can be washed away by your precious blood, but now we sincerely kneel and ask Heavenly Father to grant us peace and security. The Japanese soldiers are approaching the city, and the tragic tragedy is about to begin. Although sinful humans should suffer some torment, God! May you forgive them seventy times seven times, as the Bible says. We ask God to grant peace and security, so that sinful people have the opportunity to renew themselves, and use your spirit of love to influence the enemy's atrocities, so that the people in our city can live in peace, looking up to Heavenly Father to accept our sincere prayers, Amen."

In a brightly lit city, news came that the Chinese soldiers were safely withdrawing, and there would be satisfactory hope in the near future. Everyone's faces were filled with pride and joy. In the preparatory meeting for the celebration, the chairman said; Let us pray to God, by the grace of God, we will have the help of our warriors, so that our celebration can begin today. Comrades! Let us pray, so many people knelt down, and the prayer began··

"Heavenly Father! We thank you for giving our courage, for giving our nation a glorious history, for expanding our territory to the three eastern provinces of China. Here we want to pray that God will give our warriors great courage and strength, and quickly flatten the three eastern provinces of China, completing our wishes."

God, in the dark, received two prayers at the same time. God seemed too embarrassed to answer. Under the urgency of these two prayers, wisdom came from the middle, so he said to the first person with a soothing tone...

"Here I allow your prayers to grant you peace and security, but you must remember the saying 'Love your enemies.' You should open the city gates to love your enemies. This is the peace I give you."

God turned around and answered the second prayer...

"Remember the saying 'Love your enemies.' When your enemies open the city to love you, you should also love them."

It was difficult for God to come up with a perfect solution to solve all the problems. Hallelujah! Long live God!

A Sketch of Several Typical Characters in Shanghai

— Ju

(1) Celebrities and Tycoons

Their clothes are so shabby, yet their faces are generally greasy with fat. This is the portrait of a celebrity and tycoon. At first glance, they look just like waiters and errand boys. Therefore, they sometimes inevitably suffer the ridicule of the clueless waiters at banquets. However, celebrities and tycoons have a heaven-defying cultivation: "A gentleman does not argue about petty matters." It doesn't matter. Just explain to the blind waiter so he doesn't look down on people with shabby clothes next time. This precisely highlights their "magnanimous" demeanor, scaring the waiter into scurrying away like a rat, banging his head several times, and begging for forgiveness. And the general bystanders are in awe and praise endlessly. These celebrities and tycoons have a transcendent influence in Shanghai, tightly connected with the authorities of both Chinese and foreigners. If there are disturbances in the market, or talk of reforming the municipality, the rights and obligations of the common people are spun around in their palms. Their cars speed through the center of the street, because they rarely have time to go for a drive. They are all high-class Chinese, the big shots on the Shanghai stage.

(2) Western-Suited Youths

In Shanghai, when you mention Western-suited youths, they are as numerous as tadpoles in the rice paddies in February and March, and they jump and shout like frogs in the rice paddies in March and April. This group is extremely complex. There are young masters, company clerks, civil servants, college students, and gigolos. But under the uniform cover of Western suits (note: they are not all wearing blue suits), no one can tell their identity and duties. They have plenty of leisure time and money. They stroll in rows along the streets, which not only contributes to the hustle and bustle of the market, but is also an indispensable decoration of the metropolis. Going from amusement parks to parks, or stepping into the towering revolving door, is their daily routine. But there are also a small number who are diligently studying at the book stalls or beside the roadside news boards. Staring at the legs of passing women seems to be their only duty when they are strolling around. In Shanghai, which spans dozens of miles of foreign concessions, this group of characters is indeed indispensable.

(3) Modern Misses

Things grow by "inheriting and generating" each other. With so many Western-suited youths, there also needs to be a group of modern misses, matching yin and yang, the two sexes vying for beauty. Thus, there are so many misses, stepping on high-heeled leather shoes, galloping like horses to show off their ability to dress up. There are daughters of noble families, socialites, dancers, and female students. And so on down the line, there are female gangsters, prostitutes, and women from the salted meat shops. The wallets tightly held in their hands are so mysterious, filled with small square mirrors, lipsticks, perfume, face powder, movie brochures, and admission tickets. Their eyes don't wander, but they also don't dislike men staring at them. When passing by large companies, they will stop for a moment to see if there are any new clothing and accessories on display.

(4) Idle Young Men

They wear clothes like young masters, with the cuffs folded back halfway, silk socks, and embroidered satin shoes. That wide silk trouser belt nearly sweeps the knees. Three or five of them gather together, and they are either talking about which rotten goods are alluring, or how they scrounged up the rice for yesterday's dinner. Sometimes they take out a few copper coins from their pockets, and everyone throws them at a target. It is a way to pass the time, even though the stakes are not high. When a strange woman walks by, they follow her and offer their flattery in a couple of words, embarrassing the woman enough to call the police. This often happens on Avenue Edward VII and Yu Yuan Road. When the police arrive, they scatter in all directions, fleeing for their lives. Sometimes they will spit two mouthfuls of thick phlegm on your clean clothes for no reason. If you protest, they will say that you stepped on their embroidered satin shoes and invite you to a teahouse. And so, they have a place to spend the day.

(5) Nannies and Maids

The alley entrance and the tiger stove are where they set up shop to discuss right and wrong. With a twist of their hips, we can hear a lot of valuable news from their wrinkled lips: which young mistress has a wild man to accompany her during the day; which family is truly wealthy, changing a dozen sets of new clothes a day; which nanny is the most troubled, with many tasks and little extra money, and when she goes to buy groceries, the young mistress follows her, not allowing a single copper coin to be pocketed; while another only needs to greet the guests during mahjong games to get a thick stack of silver coins; and which young mistress is the most fierce, blinding the nanny in one eye and breaking the young maid's nose. Although they are all busy people, they can still spend an hour or two gossiping. Sometimes, if they have a lover nearby, the conversation will turn to sweet nothings. This is also a typical character in Shanghai.

Saving the Nation with Tears

People cry because of distress. Distress comes either from strong external oppression or from deep internal stimulation, which cannot be suppressed, so they resort to crying. This is a temporary or emotional impulse, and its meaning is also very great. On a small scale, it can arouse people's sympathy, and on a large scale, it can save the country from decline.

When Lin Daiyu quarrels with someone, she secretly sobs alone in her room. When Baoyu sees her, he quickly finds some gentle words to comfort her. When Miss X fails to win first place in a race, tears well up in her eyes. The students quickly take out their handkerchiefs to dry her tears. This is how crying can arouse people's sympathy.

"The wife of Qi Liang of Hua Zhou was good at crying for her husband, thereby changing the customs of the country. Wu Zixu attacked Chu with the Wu army, and Shen Baoxu entered Qin to beg for troops, leaning against the courtyard wall and crying for seven days, so the Duke of Qin sent generals to settle his country's difficulties." This is how crying can save the country from decline.

Since the September 18th Incident, the entire country has regarded saving the nation as the most urgent task. All kinds of "saving the nation with beauty," "saving the nation with dancing," "saving the nation with the Kalachakra Tantra Dharma Assembly," "saving the nation with aviation," as well as "telegrams" and "protests," have been popular for a time. As a result, the people's spirit has waned, the great powers are watching, and the enemy troops are penetrating deeper. The national salvation strategies, which were originally aimed at relieving the national crisis, have achieved such results, and one cannot help but cry out in unison: "This road is impassable!" We should change to another path! No one has yet mentioned "saving the nation with tears." I am not talented, but I will promote it to join in the fun.

The tears we need are not the tears of children like Lin Daiyu and Miss X, but the bloody tears like those of Shen Baoxu and the wife of Qi Liang. Our diplomats, in today's "weak nations have no diplomacy," are wasting their breath by arguing. It is better to go to Roosevelt or Stalin and cry bitterly, begging them to settle our national crisis. Shen Baoxu cried for seven days before the Duke of Qin was willing to send troops. Even if our diplomats cry for another seven days, they should not be impatient, as long as they can achieve the goal of sending troops.

It is feared that even with foreign aid, if we do not make efforts ourselves, the effect will be very small! Therefore, we should also send a few people to cry to the generals who possess large armies and love to play civil wars, crying until their hearts ache, and they will have no choice but to bite the bullet and go to the front line.

"Nothing is more sorrowful than the death of the heart." The general young masters and mistresses are drunk in dance halls every day, and the national crisis has long been put behind them. It is very difficult to awaken them with gentle words or vicious scolding! Sometimes it even causes them to feel resentful. Therefore, tears must be used to cleanse their minds.

Tears can indeed move people. Compatriots! Why not put it into practice?

Shop Clerk Correspondence

Several Legal Issues

Mr. Editor, my legal advisor in duty, I hereby ask you to indicate the following two matters of legal responsibility with the utmost sincerity, I am extremely grateful.

(1) I am a small staff member in a large company, and my monthly income is only enough to make ends meet, but the responsibilities I bear are not light. My family has an ancestral hall, with about 400 acres of ancestral property, which was managed by my grandfather. Due to poor management, it gradually decreased to about 200 acres. After my grandfather died, it was managed by my father, who sold another 100 acres of ancestral property. Now my father passed away last year, so I inherited and managed the ancestral hall and ancestral property (according to my family's custom, the ancestral hall and ancestral property are managed by the eldest son of the eldest branch, and have always been regarded as private property. When my father sold the ancestral property, no clansmen came out to speak). Now the existing ancestral property is only 100 acres! (About 120-130 yuan can be produced each year, which I collect and use) Now please ask...

A, If clansmen come out and order me to replenish the ancestral property to 400 acres, am I legally responsible?

B, My ancestral hall is in the countryside of Suzhou. Because there are too many petty thieves in Jiangbei, no one dares to guard it. During the "January 28th Incident" last year, when the soldiers passed by, they dismantled the wood to fill defense projects and fuel. Now the ancestral hall has collapsed and there is no strength to rebuild it. If clansmen come out and force me to rebuild it, what legal responsibility should I bear?

(2) My relatives' family was originally well-off, but due to having a prodigal son, they gradually became indebted. This spring, the business failed again, so they could not support themselves. Now they owe about 3,000 yuan. Now they have houses, goods, furniture, and means of livelihood worth about 1,500 yuan. If they declare bankruptcy, they can probably repay about 50%. Are there any other criminal liabilities (such as imprisonment, etc.) besides declaring bankruptcy? Now my relative has left. Unexpectedly, this young master also slipped away. What kind of responsibility should this matter bear in law?

That's all. I hope you will answer me directly! Thank you, thank you! Best wishes

Respectfully, Wang Tonghe

Editor's Note: Regarding the first question, it should be attributed to the bad habits. According to the investigation of the ancestral hall and ancestral property, whether it was donated by the eldest branch alone or built by the entire clan, as the name suggests, it should be owned by the entire clan; how can it be regarded as the private property of the eldest branch? Your grandfather or father has already abused their power; the elders and juniors of the entire clan have also given up asking about it. For the current plan, it seems that Mr. Wang should come forward, invite the clansmen, declare on the one hand that the ancestral property should be returned to the clansmen, and declare on the other hand that he will give up this annual income of 120-130 yuan. Regarding the matters handled by your grandfather or father, since the clansmen have already given up in advance, now they can only request ratification; regarding the matters handled by Mr. Wang, they should be reported in detail. Whether to rebuild or not is up to the public opinion of the entire clan.

Regarding the second question, your relative suffered a loss of about 3,000 gold due to having a prodigal son and business failure. After mortgaging the houses, goods, furniture, and means of livelihood, they lost about 1,500 gold. This matter can be applied to the court and handled in accordance with the bankruptcy law; if there is no concealment, they can originally not bear other criminal liabilities. However, the father and son are now both leaving, which inevitably makes people suspicious. But if the matter is factual and there is no concealment, it is still best to come forward; if there is concealment, they should announce it automatically. Otherwise, the creditors can sue the court for absconding with the money. The houses, goods, furniture, and means of livelihood will inevitably be seized; and your relatives, father and son, must be arrested and brought to justice. At that time, even if you say there is no concealment, I am afraid no one will believe it.

Film Special

From the Song "Spring River Flower Moon Night" to Emerging Music (Continued)

— Ren Xida

But now in 1933, capitalism has entered its final period of contradiction. The development of machinery has instead become a demon in the fate of capitalism. The bourgeoisie is so unable to be optimistic. Therefore, all the music that exaggerates machinery and anesthetizes humanity is no longer enough to anesthetize people, and no longer enough to represent social life and resentment. Therefore, the "jazz" music of capitalism has also entered its final period of decline with the fate of capitalism, and can no longer develop.

During this transition period, "emerging" music has not yet become widespread, and old music has lost its timeliness. At the same time, the declining European bourgeoisie no longer has the power to develop its new class art. Therefore, the petty bourgeoisie who are looking for a way out in capitalism have found the aristocratic music before capitalism. They feel that this quiet mood can still give people a little memory of happiness. Therefore, they have adopted the songs in "Spring River Flower Moon Night" and the songs in "Yaohua Village" as a kind of attempt to modernize the music of the agricultural era. So it is very obvious that this kind of music is absolutely not suitable for the needs of the modern era, so its lifespan will not be long, and it will die before the decline of capitalism.

Now movies and music are almost inseparable, and must be harmonious. Since music has changed, the same is true of motion pictures. It has shifted from films about the madness of big capitalism to silence and satire. Therefore, the knight of capitalism, "Hollywood," has also moved from the United States to Europe. But if Europe brings "Hollywood" in its entirety and continues to be the knight of capitalism fighting for territory, it will be the same as "Hollywood" in the United States, which will not work! Therefore, we know that if we want to establish a second "Hollywood" in Europe, its movies must not only not be the knight of capitalism, but also the eulogist of capitalism. What will replace all the old music in the future is the new realist, popular music. This kind of music is brand new and progressive in both form and nature. Especially in the future, as society becomes more progressive and more organized, industrialized society, the "jazz" music representing the power of machinery will not only not eliminate this feature in the form of future "emerging" music, but will also more powerfully "organize" and "popularize" it. At the same time, in terms of emotion, it must completely eliminate its "anesthetic" and replace it with the deep cry and power of the largest number of people. Establish the new emerging music art, great value and success! Replace all the individual and anesthetic music of the old era and stand alone! (The End)

Film Reviews

Review of "Heroes of Moscow"

— Ming

(Clear All Wires)

Three Russian films have been shown in Shanghai, and the themes are completely to denigrate the decline of the world economy, the collapse of assets, and social unrest, to set off the bright road of socialism. Of course, the capitalist countries are not willing to give in and want to retaliate, so "Heroes of Moscow" Clear All Wires was produced in response to the times.

This is a humorous comedy, satirizing the boredom of the Soviet Russian government and the foolishness of the people, and creating a kind of contemptuous and insulting joke from these materials. Since it is a film that considers itself humorous, we don't seem to need to delve into the irrationality of the performance.

There is meaning to the play, but it is only for the attack on socialism, promoting the "heroic spirit" of the Americans.

In this point, I feel that the original motivation is somewhat like "Unbreakable" Welcome Danger three years ago.

The story is not very special, just to say that an American reporter stationed in Moscow was fired because of the lover of the newspaper manager. So he instigated someone to kill a White Russian aristocrat, in order to use this news to plot reinstatement. Unexpectedly, the assistant misunderstood and went to kill a Red Russian police chief. He was afraid of getting into trouble, so he protected the police chief at the expense of himself. The police chief was fortunate to be unharmed, and he himself was wounded by a gun. So he was called the "Hero of Moscow" by the Red Russians, and this news raised his value. Soon, he was reinstated and married his lover to become a reporter stationed in China.

Indeed, after the success of the first five-year plan in Soviet Russia, the housing problem has not yet been solved. (See the Soviet Inspection Record) This film tightly grasped this weakness to play out, but the depiction in it was excessive, and the stupidity, incompetence, and immorality of Soviet Russian material life and Soviet Russian people, from government members to small workers, were all unbelievable. Its purpose is to make people disgusted with socialism, but the result only exposes the despicable personality of American newspaper reporters.

In terms of technique, the director could not find anything except some inexplicable jokes that wanted to delve into Soviet Russia. A few of the shots can be considered clever, and the light is not important in a comedy, and it is average here. There are more dialogues than ordinary British films, and the pronunciation is good. Most of the humorous words in the dialogue are "witty remarks" that scold Soviet Russia.

Lee Tracy, who plays the reporter, portrays the American newspaper reporter as having no backbone, really like a "dead end," and the performance is still worthy of being a "humorous star." The two female characters, BenitaHume and Una Merkel, are very ordinary, and there is nothing to recommend except for some glamorous sensuality.

The scenery is deliberately simple, writing Moscow like a ghost town. Perhaps Americans are particularly satisfied with this?

In short, it is an unusual comedy that vents its anger for capitalism and attacks Soviet Russia.

Audience Opinions

Review of "Spring Water Love Waves"

— Fang Long

From the opening of the film, we know that "Spring Water

Lilian Harvey, who is skilled in English, German, and French, has now become the darling of both Europe and the United States, but Hollywood is trying to keep her in the United States. This is her recent photo.

Love Waves" is based on the novel "Hidden Criminal," but the plot in the film is not very similar to "Hidden Criminal," and many of them have lost the original meaning of the book. This may be because the authors and screenwriters have different focuses.

The consciousness of this film is still acceptable, even if it cannot win everyone's satisfaction, at least it has pointed out the hypocrisy of snobbish marriages, the danger of reckless love, and the lessons that women who are played with should learn. Other aspects, such as the obsession with money, the obsession with officials, the local tyrants and evil gentry, the remnants of feudal forces, and the need for national unity at the end of the play, have all been given considerable play.

The most noteworthy point of the whole play is the shouting of the slogan of Northwest reclamation. The honeyed realm of the southeast and the desolation and abandonment of the border areas have formed the entire deformed weakness of China. It has a direct impact on problems such as economic collapse and rural bankruptcy. "Spring Water Love Waves" is the first to advocate saving three years of moxibustion, is this not worthy of praise?

The director is very hardworking, although he cannot find any outstanding features, the development of the whole play's plot and the rhythm of the performance can not lose the harmony of coordination, and the tense mood. In particular, the content and form are developed in a balanced and appropriate manner, and the audience's emotions are always grasped. The director's outstanding style is revealed everywhere in the grief of the victims in the play, the enlightenment of the environment of each person's awareness, the motivation of the transformation, the path of struggle, and the connection of each segment. In terms of skill, we also see considerable ingenuity, at least the director's skill is meticulous.

Speaking of the actors' performances, Hu Die has good facial expressions, and several close-ups are even more exciting. Sun Min's performance is still sincere in two scenes. Although Hu Ping's performance opportunities are few, the results are very good. Yan Yuexian is also good.

The scenery is very beautiful, and the scenery is generally good. However, the water surface of Chunshui Lake is too narrow, it is simply like a small stream, which is a fly in the ointment. The position of the lens, the photography light, etc. are all good, and the subtitles have also given considerable help.

In short, "Spring Water Love Waves" is a progressive film, which always gives the audience a good impression, although it lacks some stimulation.

An Overview of Soviet Russian Films (3)

— Written by Rudolf Messumin

(2) The Plan of the Soviet Russian Film Industry

Within the entire territory of the Soviet Union, the film industry is the most important tool for communication. Since other industries have careful and detailed plans, the film industry cannot be an exception. In the interest of facilitating film propaganda throughout the country, Soviet Russia divides the country into regions; in a broad sense, these regions are like the four poles of a compass. Within each region, there is an organization of a central production place, which is a large photography place. This large photography place has the authority to control and manage the small photography places established in various important locations in the region. And the large photography place is subordinate to the All-Union Cinema Sojus or Kint in Moscow. The All-Union Cinema Union controls the power of the national film industry; it is responsible for the economic maintenance of production places in various regions; the products of photography places in various regions are also accepted and controlled by it; and it supervises and guides the progress of affairs in various regions at any time. But in fact, the subordinate organizations in various regions enjoy a lot of freedom and are not subject to undue interference from the parent organization, and the orders issued by the parent organization are only limited to the length of films required by photography places in various regions, and there is very little interference in the content and themes of the films.

The Soviet authorities must establish a central production place in each region so that the central organization can distribute films depicting the life conditions of a certain region to other regions of the country. The life culture of the Gothozo region is very different from the life culture of the German, Volga, or Siberian regions, but the Soviet authorities firmly believe that if films depicting the life conditions of various regions can be exchanged and transported with each other, they can not only benefit the people's impressions, but also generate the idea of unity among the people and arouse the responsibility of cooperation.

They also said that allowing the residents of Turkey to see pictures of the actions of Caucasians whose lives are completely different from theirs is enough to make them feel that although the lives of races are different, they are working for socialism... In this way, the emotions of ignorance and isolation from the world that are often self-conscious by backward nations can be eliminated. In this way, the people of Turkey can realize from the film that they are not isolated, but are part of a larger plan, and are working hard for the construction of socialism, regardless of race and boundaries. As for the various fears held by these nations, such as the oppression and prohibition of special customs, etc., they can also be calmed down by the simple method of film propaganda.

(To be continued)
