Construction of Shanghai North Railway Station Commences

Architect Zhao Shen Assists in Design

丨 Zhongnan Construction Company Undertakes Construction 丨

The Refreshed New Look of Shanghai North Railway Station After Reconstruction (Drawings by the Design Department of Hua Yi Architectural Firm)

The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways previously planned to build a new station, but this was temporarily suspended due to the current situation. The original site of the North Station is now filled with dilapidated walls and ruins, which not only obstruct the view but also lack a place for passengers to rest while waiting for trains. The railway's traffic department also needs to have a station office to manage train operations. Since the new station will not be built for the time being, the renovation of the old station cannot be delayed. After the bureau submitted a request to the Ministry of Railways and obtained approval, it immediately published a public tender for construction. The bureau opened the bids publicly on the afternoon of May 1st, receiving a total of seventeen bids. As a result, Zhongnan Construction Company was deemed the most suitable and was awarded the project. It is reported that the bureau's goal in renovating the old station is to utilize the existing foundations and stone walls to create a more modern station. The entire building will have three floors, with the first and second floors serving as offices for the traffic department, and the lower floor also serving as a waiting area for passengers. Upon entering, there will be a large hall, with waiting rooms, baggage storage, a dining room, a cloakroom, a washroom, etc. on the left and right sides of the hall, all simple, beautiful, and practical. The entire project is managed by the bureau's engineering department, with architect Zhao Shen of Hua Yi Architectural Firm responsible for the internal and external layout, decoration, and construction matters. It is estimated that the project will be completed in a few months, at which time the North Station will have a completely new look.

On International-Style Architecture by Huang Yingdai

In the past ten years, many new meanings have emerged, but now they have reached a point of exhaustion. When we go to major European cities, especially in the United States, all the buildings have already been ruined by modern architecture. The so-called modernists do not refer specifically to architectural techniques. This plan uses various different new styles. They have developed a strong interest in the uniqueness of the exterior, rather than using new materials to build houses to suit issues such as tools, speed, and economy. These modernist architects can consider all aspects of the slanted or straight lines of windows and doors, black, white, and various other colored bricks, tiles, and cement, all forms and colors, shiny metals, special wood, and various decorations. And extremely pay attention to so-called modernist architects. When planning buildings, they pay great attention to the external inclined columns, but treat the internal columns that support the roof as unimportant. There are special decorations on the top of those columns, some with floral stones, some with concrete decorations, and in the middle of the windows, special iron plates or stones are also used to make everything different from the past. They assume that all the facades of the houses must be concrete or made of floral stone glass, and all the corners of the houses must be made of glass. The entrance walkways are especially unique, with imitation brick and stone forming unusual walls. Everything has a peculiar color. Modernists believe that all modern objects have unsafe characteristics in the planning of the interior construction of houses. I remember an interesting joke that happened in the market once. A modernist architect was walking by hunched over. A friend asked, "What's wrong with you? Does your back hurt?" He replied, "No, it's not a backache, it's modern objects."

So-called modern architecture, which is currently the most popular, is about building houses of different styles. Currently, it does not seek for the house itself to exist permanently, but only for the house to have a certain characteristic, and the main condition is to satisfy everything. So, what conditions must this kind of house meet? Simply put, it must meet everything modern, everything can be harmonized and unified, neat and simple, with special colors, each room will not conflict with each other, and all material and spiritual needs are met. We are no longer interested in imitating all the methods in architecture for four thousand years. It has nothing to do with us. The value it possesses no longer exists. And because of the architectural revolution, people's old ideas have been completely eliminated. Many 20th-century art architects say that in architecture, as a result of the development of industry, so-called art has already died out. And in the current era, the buildings produced in the evolution of so-called art have completely eliminated the beauty of buildings. In terms of facts, we can all see new buildings built with new materials such as steel, cement, and glass. But they don't pay much attention to art. As for ancient architecture, it is not like this. Their architecture emphasizes the spirit, and the interior decoration is especially considered an important matter. But the important qualities that modern architecture considers are completely different from the past. We are at the beginning of an era because we have the ultimate ability in technology, and now we know that architecture is in revolution and produces all kinds of forms that did not exist before. However, when new materials are adopted, human life above the standard, and human beings and industry and commerce are progressing so rapidly, what important changes will occur in architecture? When constructing houses, we use all new materials as materials. However, we still wear masks and use thousands of years of indoor decoration methods to cover up the new buildings. And there is another fallacy, pretending these houses to be a kind of modern architecture. Can these modern building materials really help us build those bank houses, train stations, and various offices, engine rooms, various private residences, and increase the beauty of the appearance? And are we all using these functions? Do we have a faithful attitude towards these buildings? However, we have a disgust for all houses that are too expensive and useless, and we have a completely faithful attitude to deal with all buildings. "

"I once found a rubber factory built in 1931 in a very famous industrial center city. The outside was built in the Egyptian style with cement, and the outside was carved with sphinxes, lotus flowers, lotus leaves, everything. Opposite half a mile away, a factory building was built with cement and steel bones. This house made people feel disgusted. Train stations, bank offices, apartments, warehouses, these houses have different styles. Some imitate ancient Greek temples, some imitate the palaces of the Nanhua, and even the churches after the revival. When we see these complicated and chaotic houses, we almost feel dizzy. Large stones or marble pillars are useless and added with ugly decorations. Paired with modern buildings, it will inevitably make people disgusted and feel the hypocrisy of architecture. So who can use new raw materials to build era buildings? Of course, our general bold engineers will take on this important mission. They have built large ocean-going ships, various offices, bank offices, and engineers have also built bridges, mine rooms, railways, oil stations, power generation rooms, power rooms, airplanes, airships, and all other modern machines. The tall multi-story buildings of the factory. The first floor is made of glass. The steel bone columns are also very thin. And 60 floors of houses can be built on top. These engineers use arithmetic methods to generate these buildings, which limit the laws of nature. And build this era architecture, which makes us feel that everything is in tune and harmonious. We are not discarding all the architectural styles of the ancient times. They are not single-mindedly imitating the houses of the Italian Renaissance. In summary, these new buildings are taking the advantages of ancient architecture and abandoning its disadvantages, and then using various new methods to apply them to the buildings of the era."

"We only need to see the grain silos and heavy-duty cranes in the United States, Canada, and Buenos Aires, etc., which are the first fruits produced in this new century. Engineers are not enthusiastically pursuing a correct theory of architecture. They are just holding a kind of cold and calm attitude. And led by a principle that controls the universe, we get a method of estimation. We only need to see the aesthetics of all modern engineering. From the automatic trains from New York to Chicago, the sleeper cars in France, the Zeppelin airships in Germany, the giant ocean-going ships in the United Kingdom, the airplanes in Italy, the tanks in Switzerland, mechanical and electrical power have made today's world form a special scene. And have the practical ability and courage to make this scene a reality. They use modern materials to build modern styles, and all the outdated, ineffective, and meaningless clichés in the old style are completely discarded. The era when the life of architecture moved on a narrow road has now reached its end. And it has reached a period of a new spirit being generated. All engineers can use clear ideas to engage in architecture, so that the buildings of the era will be produced endlessly with the era."

On Modern Architecture and Interior Decoration by Ying

In Europe and America, in the past few years, many buildings have tended towards the architectural movement of the times, based on the inherent architectural style of the country, and also imitating all architectural styles, taking the best and making up for the worst, in order to make the architecture increasingly perfect. The only reason for the emergence of this kind of building is that it is influenced by modern life. In a designated area, when we are building, everything should be in line with science, so that a house, we live inside, is like a machine, the general architect. Are carefully considering abandoning all the unnecessary decorations on the outside of the house, and the interior decorations are also the same, and striving to emphasize the economic and functional aspects. To put it plainly, it is to make the building have a great function and be suitable for economic principles. Most women are engaged in active occupations or social life. They all hope to use the least amount of effort to get the most pleasure. Just touch a mysterious key, and the things they need, hot water or cold water, hot air or cold air, either in one room or in the whole house, can be as they wish. Use electricity to light or cook. In the electric cold room, you can keep all the meals at a certain temperature. Just turn her wrist, and she can prepare a meal for the king. On the flameless electric stove, she can cook all kinds of meals, and she can take the canned food from the shelf at any time and open it to listen. The sound of electric vacuum cleaners and sewing machines, in the ears of housewives, is like the music from the radio, or the sound of piano playing, exactly the same. In a modern house, all the equipment can reduce working hours, like a typewriter, very fast, and very useful. The external form uses a logical way to determine everything, and the interior also matches the exterior in this way. If we study the problem of function in detail, then perhaps it is not in a house, the turning point of construction, and the starting point are related. The architectural raw materials used all have a natural and faithful expression, and there is no inappropriate situation for all the objects in the house, and there is no close relationship with the architectural elements.

Inside the house, the ground must be free, and the rooms must have empty spaces. The size of the area must have a considerable function. The transportation of utensils and the movement of people should save time. In the house, the empty spaces left in the bedroom and the places where housework is done should be appropriate, especially the places where sunlight shines. New construction raw materials · steel · hard · glass, and other various metals, make it possible to build a wide and bright house, and at the same time save a lot of raw materials. Compared with the previous buildings, they are very different from each other, and the previous ones are not suitable for use. In the buildings built in the past, all the walls were made wide, and the gaps in the doors and windows were made small. But what about modern architecture? This method is completely abandoned. The weight of the house is entirely placed on the pure steel bones or other bones. The ceiling and floor have no positive aspects. The floor aspect is completely supported by itself, and at the same time has the power to resist the environment, heat, cold, and the sound of the eardrum. Now we all advocate that extremely strong light should be injected from the outside, so scientists have a kind of glass, and the invention of this glass allows light to completely penetrate it, so the window has become the main element in a room. All the walls are now almost completely replaced by glass windows. If a house is built in a modern city, then we must use various methods to grasp the light. Many gaps are left for windows, so that the people who live inside can have more contact with outdoor life, and considering the current situation, this is also the general trend, which is due to the needs of modern civilization.

What is the function of modern architecture? In terms of ideal purpose, planning, and construction, it is completely consistent. All the houses are isolated properly, so that the beauty reaches a high limit, and at the same time makes the construction of the houses appropriate in weight and harmonious in structure. When general architects are building houses and planning them, they pay great attention to the issue of beauty.
